palāyitā  KubjT karālavadane tubhyaṃ māyājālaprasārike jālandharādhipatyatvaṃ bhaviṣyaty acireṇa tu  KubjT āgatya khecarīcakrāc chrīsiddhakauṇḍalīśvaraḥ aśeṣārthavido nāthaḥ sa te nātho bhaviṣyati  KubjT bhaviṣyanti karālinyo daśaiva duhitā tava bhaviṣyanty uttarānandā daśaite guṇavattarāḥ  KubjT prāticārās tu ṣaḍ bhadre bhaviṣyanty anugocare ājñānandasamekatvaṃ karālīduhitājanam  KubjT mālā uttarānandam īśānāḥ kariṣyanti yuge yuge jñānabhraṃśāvasāne tu saṃjñābhedān punaḥ punaḥ  KubjT karālī tava santāne bhaviṣyanti mamājñayā evam uktvā maheśānī gatā sahyaṃ mahāvanam  KubjT KubjT nīlasyottarabhāge tu mahocchuṣmavanāntagam parāparaṃ tu tenedaṃ pañcamaṃ pīṭhanāyakam  KubjT mātaṅginīkulāntastham ādyaṃ caivātha pañcamam tena jātaṃ jagat sarvaṃ tat sañjātaṃ kulākulam  KubjT rohati yathā bījaṃ dagdhaṃ tadvad idaṃ priye  KubjT ājñāyogaṃ kriyāmantraṃ muṣitvā yaḥ palāyate na ca tena samaṃ yāti tatraivāyāti niścitam  KubjT sa kathaṃ tiṣṭhate mūḍho bhuktodgīrṇe vapur yathā nābubhukṣā bubhukṣā vā ghṛṇī kṣīṇatanur bhavet  KubjT śubhaṃ vā aśubhaṃ vātha kurvāṇaṃ na hased gurum hasanād dhvaṃsam āyāti hasite hiṃsito hi saḥ  KubjT sāmānyapratipattyā vā na vaded guruṇā saha mukhe hastaṃ pradattvā tu dadādeśam iti bruvan  KubjT aṅgarakṣā na kartavyā na śāṭhyaṃ guruṇā saha uktānukteṣu kāryeṣu upekṣāṃ naiva kārayet  KubjT śaṭhas tu duṣṭabhāvaś ca mṛṣāvādyapravādakaḥ antaraṅgī na sadbhāvī sa naṣṭaḥ kañjinī yathā  KubjT dvidhābhāvābhipannasya bhinnabhāva itas tataḥ ya evaṃ vartate mūḍhaḥ sa naṣṭaḥ kañjikaṃ yathā  KubjT ājñāsphurantam ānandaṃ guruṃ tyaktvānyam āśrayet sanniruddhas tu sarvatra rājyabhraṣṭo yathā nṛpaḥ  KubjT śarīraṃ dravyavijñānaṃ vastravāhanabhūṣaṇam gurvarthaṃ dhārayed yas tu sa vai saṃskāram arhati  KubjT gurur mānyo guruḥ pūjyaś cārādhyo guravaḥ sadā gurau santoṣite sarvaṃ toṣitaṃ sacarācaram  KubjT guroḥ samo naiva hi martyaloke tathā viśeṣeṇa tu cāntarikṣe yas tārayed duḥkhamahārṇavaughāt kiṃ tasya kartuṃ sa karoti śiṣyaḥ  KubjT na mātā na pitā caiva na bhrātā naiva bāndhavāḥ upakāraṃ hi kurvanti kurute yādṛśaṃ guruḥ  KubjT evaṃ matvā varārohe duḥkhe duḥkhī sukhe sukhī guror vairodhikaṃ sthānaṃ pramādād api na vrajet  KubjT upaviṣṭasya pārśve tu kartavyaṃ mārjanādikam bhikṣāpātraṃ nivedyeta puṣpadhāṭīṃ vahet sadā  KubjT antaraṅgaṃ na kartavyaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmaṇā yat kiñcid gurave kāryaṃ tat kartavyam aśaṅkitaiḥ  KubjT ya evaṃ vartate śiṣyaḥ sukhaduḥkhasamāśrayī tasya siddhir na dūrasthā mokṣaḥ svādhīnatāṃ gataḥ  KubjT guruṇāpāditaṃ sarvam upadeśaṃ prapūjayet tasmād evaṃ viditvā tu gurur devo na cānyathā  KubjT triṣkālaṃ praṇipātena dhyānayogena taṃ yajet adṛṣṭavigraheśānam upalabhyeta nānyathā  KubjT mantradhyānatapopāyaiś caryāyogair anekadhā na paśyanti paraṃ śambhuṃ yāvan nopāsayed gurum  KubjT dhyāyanto pi sadā bhaktyā madrūpaṃ guruṇoditam tathāpi na bhavet saukhyaṃ śāmbhavaṃ paramārthataḥ  KubjT yāvan mūrdhnopari pādā ājñāyuktaḥ subhāvitaḥ tāvan na jāyate śīghram adṛṣṭaguṇalakṣaṇam  KubjT gururūpavidhau yadi niścalatā tad upāsati mūrdhni dhṛtāṅghriyugam acireṇa bhavaty upaladbhiguṇā aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakaśambhupadam  KubjT ājñāhīne parokṣatvaṃ trayāṇāṃ darśitaṃ mayā rudrabhairavavīrāṇāṃ kathanād yogaḥ pravartate  KubjT siddhe siddhaṃ vinirdiṣṭaṃ pratyakṣaguṇalakṣaṇam ājñātaḥ sampravarteta sā cājñā guravo viduḥ  KubjT śāstre śāstre smṛtaṃ jñānaṃ mayānekavidhānataḥ pratyakṣamantranihitā siddhājñā siddhagocare  KubjT tenedaṃ siddhasantānaṃ gurudevopalakṣitam yasya cājñānipātena sambodhaḥ śāmbhavo bhavet  KubjT pratyakṣaṃ guravaṃ tyaktvā jñānarūpaṃ kuleśvaram katham ārādhanānyatra kurute mohitātmanaḥ  KubjT nirvāṇāgnau jvaladdīpte yo nyatrāgnau vrajet kudhīḥ devāgāraṃ guruṃ tyaktvā vrajaty adhobhavaṃ tu saḥ  KubjT pūrvakarmaviśuddhasya śaktipātaḥ sunirmalaḥ tīvraśaktinipāto sya śīghram eva prapadyate  KubjT malakāyaprapūrṇasya mandaṃ mandaṃ pravartate abhāgyasyāpi ṣaṇmāsāt tīvratvaṃ samprapadyate  KubjT yāvan na sarvabhāvena martyalokam upāgatam gurumūrtidharaṃ śambhuṃ tāvat pāto na śāmbhavaḥ  KubjT madvīryaḥ pārado yadvat patitaḥ sphuṭitaḥ kaṇaiḥ tadvac ca deśikendrāṇāṃ rūpeṇa prabhramāmy aham  KubjT mama vīryaprasūtās te ācāryāḥ sūtakeva hi vindhanti saṃskṛtāḥ santo bhaktyoṣadhisujāraṇāt  KubjT aham ekaḥ kulālo vai khecarādau guṇojjvalaḥ sṛjāmi nikhilaṃ sarvaṃ gurutve saṃvyavasthitaḥ  KubjT sādākhyaḥ khecarāṇāṃ ca piṅgo haṃ pavanodbhavaḥ tejase nantarūpo haṃ nugrahīśo jalodbhavaḥ  KubjT śrīkaṇṭho haṃ nivṛttyante kulīśo haṃ kṣitītale nughrahāmy akhilaṃ sarvam eko py anekadhā sthitaḥ  KubjT yena yena hi bhāvena pṛcchito haṃ yathā yathā tathā tathā mayā sarvaṃ gurutve sampradarśitam  KubjT atraiva siddhasantāne pratyakṣo haṃ vyavasthitaḥ gurumūrtau sthito nityaṃ yasyājñā sampravartate  KubjT suvarṇasya yathākārāḥ saṃjñābhedair anekadhā kaṭakaṅkaṇakeyūraiḥ kaṇṭhīmudrāṅgulīyakaiḥ  KubjT tathā te guravo jñeyā mamājñāṅgasamudbhavāḥ rasavad vedhakā jñeyā stokaṃ stokaṃ bahuṃ bahum  KubjT palakoṭipalānāṃ ca guñjād evaṃ na saṃśayaḥ evaṃ vibhūtir ākhyātā yugarūpānusāriṇī  KubjT palena vihito vedhaḥ kiṃ guñjāto na vidhyati saṃskāre sati sarvatra bahustokaṃ na cintayet  KubjT parāparavibhāgena kālabhāvavaśena ca bahustokaṃ na mantavyaṃ pratyayaś cātra kāraṇam  KubjT rasaviddhaṃ yathā tāmraṃ na bhūyas tāmratāṃ vrajet ājñāviddhas tathāpy evaṃ na saṃsāram anukramet  KubjT sā cājñā vidyate yasya mama tulyaḥ kujāmbike palamātraraso bhavyaṃ guñjāmātrarasena kim  KubjT palamātraraso hy ahaṃ guñjāmātras tatodbhavaḥ evaṃ matvā gurūṇāṃ ca na vikalpo vibhūtaye  KubjT ājñāto bhukti muktiś ca sarvaṃ sādhayate kṣaṇāt vāñchitaṃ labhate sarvaṃ yadi bhaktiḥ suniścalā  KubjT ājñā tu dvividhā proktā sādhakānugrahātmikā samarthācārayuktasya tatas tāṃ tu pramocayet  KubjT prāthamikasya yā ājñāsā viśuddhiprabodhikā adhikāranimittārthaṃ punaś cājñāṃ daded guruḥ  KubjT ājñāmātreṇa santuṣṭo anyasyājñāṃ dadāti ca nehatre tu sukhaṃ tasya paratre bādhyate tu saḥ  KubjT vācāsiddhiḥ purakṣobhaṃ yāvaj jñātaṃ na yoginaḥ tāvan na kārayed dīkṣām ity ājñā pārameśvarī  KubjT jñātvāmnāyaṃ varārohe divyādivyair niṣevitam catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ catuḥ  KubjT ślokadvādaśakaṃ cānyat pañcaratnaṃ satadgraham ṣoḍhānyāsakramaṃ jñātvā etat sarvaṃ vidhānataḥ  KubjT sa yogyaḥ kramiko śiṣyo anyathā nāmadhārakaḥ tataḥ prabhṛti siddho sau pūjyaḥ pūjāpakaḥ smṛtaḥ  KubjT etadguṇaviśiṣṭo yaṃ śiṣyaḥ sarvārthadāyakaḥ mahadanyāyasamprāpto gurus taṃ na tiraskaret  KubjT evaṃ gurutvam āpnoti siddhāmnāye kujeśvari anyathā jīvikārthaṃ tu ātmānaṃ ca viḍambitaḥ  KubjT ājñāyā guṇam aiśvaryaṃ yasya jātaṃ yaśasvini tasmāt sampadyate sarvaṃ yadi dattā prasādataḥ  KubjT krameṇa vihitā cājñā ājñāmoghakramaṃ viduḥ te jyeṣṭhāḥ kramasantāne yady eṣāṃ nukramo na hi  KubjT kiṃ tu maṇḍalayogyās te na bhavanti kuleśvarāḥ candanākṣatadīpānāṃ nārhatvaṃ ca bhajanti te  KubjT adhikārājñā prathamā prasādājñā dvitīyakā sā yadi kramaśaḥ prāptā sakramānukrameṇa tu  KubjT tatra kālaṃ samārabhya gurutvaṃ bhajate tu saḥ sa yatra tiṣṭhate deśe tatra ye nye tu kanyasāḥ  KubjT bhrātṝṇāṃ bhrātṛputrāś ca tatputrāś ca gurur yathā pūjayanty avikalpena siddhimārge vidhir hy ayam  KubjT ārādhyas tiṣṭhate yatra tatra kiñcin na kārayet mantratantrakriyāyogam adhikāraṃ prabhutvatā  KubjT pañcayojanamātreṇa gatvā karma samārabhet tatpure dāsavat tiṣṭhed ājñāśravaṇatatparaḥ  KubjT svapurasthaṃ prayatnena yadārādhyaṃ na paśyati bhuñjate mohitātmānaḥ kilbiṣaṃ bhuñjate tu saḥ  KubjT prāyaścittaṃ cared devi kubjikāyāyutadvayam atha ced darpamūḍhas tu jñātvā bhuñjaty aśaṅkitaḥ  KubjT lakṣaṃ japtvā bhavec chuddhir gurupūjā tv anantaram samapādena cāruhya guror agre ajānataḥ  KubjT kubjikāyutam ekaṃ tu śudhyate gurupūjayā guror āsthānasaṃsthāne cāruhya pādukaiḥ saha  KubjT gurudṛṣṭigate pāde japate tasya pūrvavat jyeṣṭho bhrātā guror mātā guroḥ sthānārcakās tu ye  KubjT trīṇy etās tatsamā jñeyā draṣṭavyā guruvad yathā apamānya yadā hy etān ātmasambhāvitaḥ kudhīḥ  KubjT prāyaścittī salakṣeṇa śudhyate gurupūjayā upamardya guroḥ sthānaṃ pāpātmā yatra tiṣṭhati  KubjT tasya darśanasambhāṣāt pātakino bhavanti te yadā sādhuḥ prasannātmā tadā lakṣatrayeṇa vai  KubjT maṇḍalānāṃ sahasreṇa gurupūjā tv anantaram pādukopānahau chattraṃ śayyāpaṭṭo tha bhājanam  KubjT pādena saṃspṛśed yas tu śire dhṛtvāṣṭakaṃ japet  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate manthānabhedapracāraratisaṅgamo nāma tṛtīyaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrīkubjikā uvācatṛptāhaṃ devadeveśa bījamantrair anekadhā cakraiś ca vividhākāraiḥ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaiḥ  KubjT adyāpi saṃśayo nātha mantrāṇāṃ nirṇayaṃ prati pūrvaṃ ca kathitā mantrāḥ saptakoṭir asaṅkhyayā  KubjT sādhanāni punas teṣāṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakāḥ kliṣyanti manujātyantaṃ japahomaparāyaṇāḥ  KubjT vrataiś ca vividhākāraiḥ kaṣṭaiś cāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ kimarthaṃ te na sidhyanti japtvā koṭiśatair api  KubjT tvaṃ ca devo vibhuḥ kartā tvayoktaṃ sat yam ucyate avicāreṇa tad grāhyaṃ mithyā kiṃ deva bhāṣitam  KubjT dhvaṃsitāś ca tvayā lokā māyārūpeṇa bhairava  KubjT śrībhairava uvācasādhu sādhu mahāprājñe vastucodyavikalpini ye mayā kathitā mantrāḥ pūrvaṃ ye kāmasiddhidāḥ  KubjT te gopitā mayā devi varṇarūpāḥ prakāśitāḥ tena te na prasidhyanti japtvā koṭiśatair api  KubjT oṃkāreṇa tu te guptā namaskāreṇa bhāmini tena guptena guptās te śeṣā varṇās tu kevalāḥ  KubjT ekākṣarā dvyakṣarāś ca catuḥpañcanavākṣarāḥ kūṭamantrāś ca ye kecit piṇḍamantrās tathaiva ca  KubjT ekāśītipadāś cānye sahasrāntāḥ śatārdhikāḥ sarve te niṣphalāḥ proktāḥ kiṃ tu jīvavivarjitāḥ  KubjT loke prasiddham evaṃ hi jīvahīnā mṛtāḥ kila mṛtasya copacāreṇa kiṃ teṣāṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet  KubjT evaṃ mantrā varārohe akṣarārthe vyavasthitāḥ vratacaryair na sidhyanti sat yam etad udāhṛtam  KubjT sidhyante jīvayuktās tu kim atra pravicāryate anyonyavalitāś caiva bheditā dvādaśasvaraiḥ  KubjT rañjitāḥ śaktibījena sidhyante varavarṇini uktāḥ kāmapradāḥ sarve sarve cāmoghaśaktayaḥ  KubjT śivavaktrodbhavāḥ sarve mananatrāṇadharmiṇaḥ trāṇaṃ tu rakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ tac ca varṇavivarjitam  KubjT śuddhasphaṭikasakāśaṃ cāroccāravivarjitam jvalantaṃ svena tejena hṛtpadme saṃvyavasthitam  KubjT bhāvayec chūnyam ātmānam ekībhūtaṃ tayā saha suṣumṇācārayogena udyantaṃ ravibimbavat  KubjT ojāpūkākramān bhittvā vidyākubjapade sthitam tāvat kampaty asau yogī stobham āyāti tatkṣaṇāt  KubjT mudrā mantraṃ tathā bhāṣā sarvaṃ jānāti tattvataḥ kubjīśānapadaṃ prāptaṃ suptāvasthā prajāyate  KubjT īṣanmātraṃ vijānāti suptāvasthāvyavasthitaḥ brahmarandhragatā cājñā kāṣṭhavat tiṣṭhate tadā  KubjT yavamātrapramāṇaṃ tu trikoṇākṛtim uttamam vaḍavāmaṇīndriyaṃ yadvan mīlanonmīlanāni ca  KubjT tatra madhye gataṃ cetaḥ kāṣṭhāvasthā tu jāyate bherīmṛdaṅgaśabdādyair gītavādyair anekadhā  KubjT na śṛṇoti na paśyeta na cānyaṃ manyate prabhum khaḍgacakrādibhiḥ śastraiś chidyamāno na vindati  KubjT īṣanmātraṃ vijānāti śaktyāvasthā varānane śaktyantaṃ tu yadā prāptas tadā cotpatate kṣaṇāt  KubjT evaṃ krameṇa deveśi śaktyuccāraṃ samabhyaset satatābhyāsayogena vāgīśatvaṃ prajāyate  KubjT māsam ekaṃ yadābhyastaṃ kāvyakartā na saṃśayaḥ dvibhir māsair vapuṣmantaḥ kṣuttṛṣṇādyair na bādhyate  KubjT vicared akhilān lokān yāvadābhūtasamplavam akṣarārthena ye mantrās teṣām eva vidhiḥ sphuṭam  KubjT śrīkubjikā uvācaakṣarārthopadeśaś ca sampradāyaś ca kaulikaḥ yathā vijñāyate deva prasādaṃ kuru bhairava  KubjT śrībhairava uvācaśṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi mantrāṇāṃ nirṇayaṃ sphuṭam prastārādiranekaiś ca ye mantrāś coditāḥ priye  KubjT akṣarārthena te jñeyāḥ khaṇḍamantrāḥ śivoditāḥ rañjakena samāyuktā upadeśaḥ surārcite  KubjT sampradāyo bhaved devi so pi ṣaṭsu prabhedataḥ pallavo yogarodhaś ca sampuṭo grathanas tathā  KubjT vidarbhaś ca ṣaḍ ete hi sampradāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ mālinī śabdarāśiś ca kauliko vidhir uttamaḥ  KubjT sā tu jñeyā varārohe bhedāḥ pañcāśa suvrate kulaṃ tu ṣaḍvidhaṃ jñeyaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  KubjT paraṃ bījaṃ tathā mūlam āgamo vidhir eva ca varṇarāśisamāyuktaḥ ṣaḍvidhas tu kulakramaḥ  KubjT sakalo niṣkalaś caiva tathā sakalaniṣkalaḥ sūkṣmo bhinnakalaś caiva kalātīto varānane  KubjT ṣaṭprakāro bhaven mantro jñātavyaḥ siddhim icchatā śuddhadvandvajasaṭkīrṇa upadeśas tribhedataḥ  KubjT śrīkubjikā uvācasūcitā mantramārge tu ye mantrā lakṣaṇānvitāḥ te jñeyās tvatprasādena dhyānadhāraṇayogataḥ  KubjT kulamārgagatā deva yathā bhavati tat katham kathaṃ tu pallavo yoga ādi ṣaṭsu prakārataḥ  KubjT kaulikaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ kiṃ tu mantrāṇāṃ ṣaḍvidhā gatiḥ trividhaś copadeśaś ca etad icchāmi veditum  KubjT śrībhairava uvācapallavo ādideśe tu yogo madhye vijānataḥ rodhas tu ādimadhyānte sampuṭaś cādirantagaḥ  KubjT grathanaṃ cāntare jñeyam akṣarākṣarayogataḥ vidarbho mantramādau tu mantrānte vīranāyike  KubjT mālāgrathanam etad dhi jñātavyaṃ mantravādinā pallavo mantrabodhe tu yogo jñeyas tu sarvadā  KubjT amalīkaraṇe caiva sandhānasya vidhau priye yogas tu kathito hy evaṃ rodhaś caivānukathyate  KubjT tīvramantrapadastambhe vākstambhe sainyastambhane hastyādiśakaṭayantre nāvānte ca prakīrtitaḥ  KubjT teṣu rodhaḥ praśasyeta paśūnām utkrameṣu ca sampuṭo mantrarakṣāsu vaśyārthe caiva yojayet  KubjT amṛtīkaraṇe caiva viṣe sthāvarajaṅgame śāntikādiṣu kāryeṣu sampuṭas tu praśayate  KubjT grathanaṃ rūpakāryeṣu ākṛṣṭyādiṣu karmasu sandhāne tu varārohe grathanaṃ samudāhṛtam  KubjT vidarbhaḥ sarvakāryeṣu uktānukteṣu vastuṣu kartavyaṃ satataṃ devi yadi siddhiṃ samīhate  KubjT etad devi samākhyātaṃ sampradāyavidhiḥ śubhaḥ na mayā kasyacit khyātaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ gaṇāmbike  KubjT sāmprataṃ kulamārgas tu yathā bhavati tac chṛṇu paraṃ binduḥ samākhyāto hṛtpadme suranāyike  KubjT grahaṇaṃ tasya copāyas taṃ jñeyaṃ kaulikaṃ param bījaṃ kuṇḍalinī śaktir yā karoti gamāgamam  KubjT tasyāntaṃ tu tato jñātvā bījaṃ kaulikam uttamam mūlaṃ śaktiḥ smṛtā kubjī jagataḥ kāraṇātmikā  KubjT tasyā jātam aśeṣaṃ tu ābrahmabhuvanāntikam sṛjate yena suśroṇi kāryakāraṇayogataḥ  KubjT jñeyā dharmiṇi dharmitvaṃ yathoṣmā kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ etat kaulikam ākhyātaṃ mūlasaṃjñā varānane  KubjT āgamas tatra sūtrārtho vidhis tatraiva coditā varṇarāśikramo jñeyo nādiphāntasvarūpataḥ  KubjT ādikṣāntaś ca deveśi śabdarāśikramo viduḥ etat kaulikam ākhyataṃ ṣaṭprakāraṃ varānane  KubjT sakalādikrameṇaiva vakṣyamānaṃ nibodhata brahmasthaḥ sakalo mantra aṣṭatriṃśatkalair yutaḥ  KubjT pūryaṣṭakasamopeta udbhavastho vijānataḥ kaṇṭhastho niṣkalo devi kalākālavivarjitaḥ  KubjT rudrasthānagato bhadre mantro bhāvair dvibhir yutaḥ sthūlajālakalair yukto bindvādīnāṃ ca sambhavaiḥ  KubjT sūkṣmādhārasthito hy ekaḥ sparśākhyo mantravedakaḥ sakalo niṣkalaś cāsau mantro jñeyas tu suvrate  KubjT vilīno bindudeve tu yonyākārasvarūpataḥ śabdasparśavinirmukto mantro jñeyas tu niṣkalaḥ  KubjT sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataro devi sa ca sūkṣmo nigadyate kālarūpaḥ smṛto bindus taṃ bhittvā vrajate yadi  KubjT ūrdhvapade pravṛttasya suṣumṇādhāragocaraḥ pralīnaḥ śabdadeve tu cicchaktipratibodhitaḥ  KubjT bhinnakalaḥ smṛto hy evaṃ layātītas tu mokṣadaḥ pañcāvasthā samākhyātā mantrāṇām amitaujasām  KubjT yāvad evaṃ na vindeta tāvat siddhiḥ kuto bhavet hṛtkaṇṭhatālujihvauṣṭhau dantanāsodbhavākṣarāḥ  KubjT kṣaṇapradhvaṃsino devi yathotpattis tathā kṣayaḥ  kṛtakā hy acetanā śūnyā anityā jalpakārakāḥ  KubjT pañcāvasthāprabhinnas tu tadā mantram ihocyate evaṃ mantragatiṃ jñātvā sidhyante līlayā narāḥ  KubjT udbhave śuddham ity ukto viśleṣe dvandvajaḥ smṛtaḥ saṅkīrṇe layasaṃsthā hi upadeśas tridhā smṛtaḥ  KubjT sparśanaṃ cāvalokaṃ ca sambhāṣaṃ cātmadarśanam svayamāveśanaṃ caiva saṅkrāntiḥ pañcalakṣaṇā  KubjT sparśanaṃ hṛdisaṃsthaṃ tu ālokaṃ kaṇṭhadeśataḥ tālusthāne tu sambhāṣaṃ darśanaṃ bindumadhyataḥ  KubjT svayamāveśanaṃ devi kubjirandhre na saṃśayaḥ sparśane kampanaṃ jñeyam āloke dhunanaṃ bhavet  KubjT sambhāṣe tu bhavet stobhaḥ śāstrārthaṃ caiva manyate darśanena guṇāvāptir aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam  KubjT svayamāviśane devi utpaten nātra saṃśayaḥ evaṃ mantragatiṃ jñātvā sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  KubjT ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mantroddhāraṃ varānane sugupte bhūsame śuddhe gomayenopalepite  KubjT puṣpaprakaragandhāḍhye gahvaraṃ tu samālikhet saptatrayodaśair bhāgaiḥ ṣaḍ lopyāḥ ṣaṭkrameṇa tu  KubjT yathā caivaikapārśve tu dvitīyam evam eva hi ekaṃ trīṇi tathā pañca sapta nava tathaiva ca  KubjT ekādaśa tathāpy evaṃ trayodaśāvasānataḥ pañcāśad ūnam ekena kartavyaṃ hi yathāvidhi  KubjT kāmarūpād akārādau likhed evaṃ krameṇa tu svarāḥ sparśā yathāvṛttyā yāvan madhyam upāgatāḥ  KubjT oḍḍiyānagataṃ devi haṃsākhyaṃ tu mahātmanam kaṣākhyaṃ mantrarājānaṃ saṃyogena tu jāyate  KubjT evaṃ nyāse kṛte devi uddharen mālinīṃ śubhām nādiphāntakrameṇaiva yathā bhavati tac chṛṇu  KubjT padhamadhye śikhā jñeyā adhaḥśiravyavasthitā epūrvākṣaracatuṣkaṃ śiromālā nigadyate  KubjT aiśamadhye śiro devyāḥ kārayec chubhalakṣaṇam tṛtīyaṃ nayanaṃ devyā ṅachamadhyagataṃ punaḥ  KubjT nadamadhyagataṃ jñeyaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ varānane nayanau ca smṛtau devyāḥ kramād dakṣiṇavāmagau  KubjT ṭapūrve nāsikā jñeyā saṃsṛṣṭā caiva madhyagā ḍhatamadhyagataṃ gṛhya dvirabhyāsapaderitam  KubjT ṭhaḍapūrvau yutau dhastād bhūṣaṇau karṇayoḥ smṛtau vāmadakṣiṇamārgeṇa karṇabhūṣasthitāv iha  KubjT sacamadhyagataṃ vaktraṃ devyāyā vīranāyike visargāntakhamadhyasthaṃ kagamadhyagataṃ punaḥ  KubjT khapaścimaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ paścimottaram eva ca ghacamadhyagataṃ caiva uddhared akṣaraṃ śubham  KubjT ete pañca smṛtā varṇā devyā daśanakalpanā ñapūrve rasanā devyā jhaūrdhvena sarasvatī  KubjT satamadhyasthitaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ machamadhyagatoddharet ramamadhyagataṃ tadvad akṣarau tu śubhātmakau  KubjT śikharau tau smṛtau bhadre vāmadakṣiṇagau śubhau ūḍhamadhyagataṃ gṛhya ḍaṇamadhye dvitīyakam  KubjT vāmadakṣiṇagau dvau tu bāhū devyāḥ surārcite ṭaḍamadhyagataṃ caiva dvidhābhūtaṃ tu kārayet  KubjT karatalau smṛtau devyāḥ savyāsavyau vijānataḥ jamapūrvau tu aṅgulyau vāmadakṣiṇagau śubhau  KubjT aṃkamadhye karapṛṣṭhe dvidhābhūtaṃ prakalpayet ñaṭhamadhyagataṃ gṛhya vāmahaste pradāpayet  KubjT ūrdhvavaktrakapālaṃ tu amṛtākhyena pūritam dakṣiṇe tu kare jñeyaṃ yaḍhamadhye tu daṇḍakam  KubjT śūlasya kathitaṃ bhadre uddhāreṇa samuddhṛtam achamadhyagataṃ śūlam uttānam ūrdhvavaktragam  KubjT jñātavyaṃ tu vipaścidbhir yathālakṣaṇalakṣitam ghanamadhye tu hṛdayaṃ devyāyāḥ sarvakāmadam  KubjT maṣamadhyagataṃ gṛhya ātmabījaṃ śivātmakam visargasahitaṃ bhadre uddhṛtaṃ mantram uttamam  KubjT yasamadhyagataṃ prāṇaṃ devyāyā vīranāyike jacamadhyagataṃ gṛhya ravasandhigataṃ tathā  KubjT vāmadakṣiṇagau dvau tu akṣarau tau stanātmakau jhapūrve tu payo jñeyam amṛtaṃ ca udāhṛtam  KubjT nasamadhyagataṃ gṛhya udaram uddhṛtaṃ naghe kaṣākhyaṃ tattvarājānaṃ nābhiṃ devyāḥ prakalpayet  KubjT bhañamadhyagataṃ devi nitambaṃ sakalātmakam vaṣamadhyagataṃ guhyam aupaścimasamanvitam  KubjT ūrvākāraṃ bhaved bījaṃ ṇathamadhyagataṃ naghe ṇatadakṣiṇagau bījau jānunī dve prakalpayet  KubjT savyāsavyagatau jñeyau krameṇaiva śubhekṣaṇe thadadakṣiṇagau dvau tu jaṅghau dve vāmadakṣiṇau  KubjT thadamadhyagataṃ devi pabamadhyaṃ tathaiva ca dvau bījau coddhṛtau bhadre pādau jñeyau vipaścitā  KubjT vāmadakṣiṇagau proktau lakṣaṇena samanvitau evaṃ samyagvidhānena uddhṛtā mālinī priye  KubjT sapta koṭyas tu vidyānāṃ mantrāṇām amitaujasām eṣā hy ekā parā yonir mālinī sarvakāmadā  KubjT mālayitvā sthitā yena tenaiṣā mālinī smṛtā ye bhūtā ye bhaviṣyanti aprameyā varānane  KubjT rudrāṇāṃ yoginīnāṃ ca sā mātaiva nigadyate avarṇā varṇasaṃyogā jñātavyā tu śubhekṣaṇe  KubjT sarvarudrātmakā mantrā rudrāḥ śaktyātmakāḥ priye śaktis tu mātṛkā jñeyā sā jñeyā tu śivātmikā  KubjT evaṃ mantrapramāṇaṃ tu kathitaṃ tava śobhane etad ādyaṃ samākhyātaṃ gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ  KubjT ekavīravidhānaṃ tu prāg uktam anya āgame  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate mantranirṇayagahvaramālinyuddhāro nāma caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrībhairava uvācaumāmāheśvaraṃ cakraṃ kathayāmi suniścitam padaṃ ca padabhedaṃ ca yo jānāti sa sidhyati  KubjT aiṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya padaṃ caiva daśākṣaram namaś cāmuṇḍe dvitīyaṃ syāt pañcākṣaram udāhṛtam  KubjT namaś cākāśamātṝṇāṃ padam anyat tṛtīyakam aṣṭākṣaraṃ samākhyātaṃ lakṣaṇena vilakṣitam  KubjT sarvakāmārthasādhakīnāṃ padaṃ caiva caturthakam navākṣaram idaṃ devi padaṃ yat samudāhṛtam  KubjT ajarāmarīṇāṃ padaṃ cātra kathitaṃ pañcaguṇāvaham akṣarāṇāṃ samāsena rasasaṅkhyā udāhṛtā  KubjT sarvatrāpratihatagatīnāṃ padaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ varānane daśākṣaraṃ samākhyātaṃ kathitaṃ vīranāyike  KubjT svarūpapararūpaparivartanīnāṃ padaṃ saptamakaṃ bhavet akṣarāṇāṃ samāsena daśatritayam uttamam  KubjT sarvasattva vaśīkaraṇocchādanonmūlanasamastakarmapravṛttīnāṃ padaṃ cāṣṭamakaṃ bhavet akṣarāṇāṃ samāsena viṃśaccatvārisaṅkhyayā  KubjT sarvamātṛguhyahṛdayaparamasiddhaṃ padaṃ tu navamaṃ bhavet akṣarāṇāṃ samāsena śakrasaṅkhyā varānane  KubjT parakarma tathā devi chedanakaraṃ prakīrtitam siddhikaraṃ ca evātra padaṃ caiva dvipañcakam  KubjT akṣarāṇāṃ tathā saṅkhyā ekatra samudāhṛtā dvisaptaparimāṇena sphuṭam etat kuleśvari  KubjT śṛṇu cānyaṃ varārohe mātṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ śubham akṣarāṇāṃ pramāṇena dvicatuṣkaṃ varānane  KubjT ekādaśamam etad dhi padaṃ sarvaguṇāvaham tad yatheti samārabhya dvitīyaṃ śobhanaṃ priye  KubjT brahmāṇīti padaṃ pūrvaṃ māheśvarī dvitīyakam kaumārīti tṛtīyaṃ syād vaiṣṇavyā tu caturthakam  KubjT vārāhyā pañcamaṃ jñeyam aindrī ṣaṣṭhamakaṃ bhavet aiśānī saptamaṃ proktam āgneyī cāṣṭamaṃ priye  KubjT evamādyāḥ sthitā devyaḥ kathitās tava śobhane aghore amoghe varade vicce vai vacanaṃ śubham  KubjT sarvāsāṃ caiva mātṝṇāṃ svāhāpraṇavasaṃyutam aiṃ cāmuṇḍe padaṃ pūrvam ūrdhvakeśi dvitīyakam  KubjT jvalitaśikhe tṛtīyaṃ tu vidyujjihve caturthakam tārakākṣi tathā devi pañcamaṃ parikīrtitam  KubjT piṅgalabhruve nāmena ṣaṣṭhamaṃ tu sulocane vikṛtadaṃṣṭre padaṃ hy etat saptamaṃ parikīrtitam  KubjT kruddhe ti ca tathā cānyam aṣṭamaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam māṃsaśoṇitasurāsavapriye navamaṃ daśamaṃ tu hasadvayam  KubjT nṛtyadvayaṃ tathā coktaṃ daśamekaṃ tu suvrate vijṛmbha ca tathā yugmaṃ daśadve ca prakāśitam  KubjT māyātrailokyarūpeti daśatritayam uttamam sahasraparivartanīnāṃ dvisaptamaṃ parameśvari  KubjT nudayugmaṃ tripañcaiva kūṭayugmaṃ dviraṣṭakam ciriyugmaṃ tathā bhadre daśasapta ca ekataḥ  KubjT hiridvitayam ekatra daśaaṣṭa śubhekṣaṇe bhiri caiva dvirabhyāsād viṃśamekonasaṅkhyayā  KubjT trāsanidvitayaṃ caiva padaṃ viṃśamakaṃ bhavet bhrāmaṇiyugmam etad dhi viṃśamekaṃ tu uttamam  KubjT vidrāvaṇi dvirabhyāsād viṃśadvayaṃ tathānaghe kṣobhaṇīti dvirabhyāsād viṃśatrikam udāhṛtam  KubjT māraṇidvitayaṃ caiva viṃśacatvārisaṅkhyayā sañjīvanipade dve tu pañcaviṃśapadaṃ priye  KubjT heriyugmaṃ smṛtaṃ bhadre ṣaḍviṃśakam anuttamam geriyugmaṃ tathā proktaṃ saptaviṃśatimaṃ padam  KubjT ghuri caiva dvirabhyāsād aṣṭāviṃśa varānane ghurileti tathāpy evam ūnatriṃśam udāhṛtam  KubjT namo mātṛgaṇāyeti triṃśakaṃ kathitaṃ sphuṭam namo namaḥ aiṃ vicce svāhā triṃśam ekottaraṃ padam  KubjT samastapadasaṃyogāt parimāṇaṃ śatārdhakam varṇānāṃ ca śate dve tu dvānavatyā varānane  KubjT adhikaṃ kathitaṃ bhadre mātṝṇāṃ nāmavarjitam padabhedas tu vidyāyā jñātavyaḥ sādhakena tu  KubjT prayatnena varārohe tantrāmnāyaprapālakaḥ sakṛd uccāritā vidyā samayajño bhavaty asau  KubjT pañcapraṇavamuddhāraṃ yathā tvaṃ gahvare śṛṇu eomadhye samuddhṛtya bindunādamalaṅkṛtam  KubjT bhagākhyaṃ prathamaṃ bījam uddhṛtaṃ paramākṣaram vaṣamadhyagataṃ gṛhya ṇaṭamadhyāsane sthitam  KubjT iumadhyena sambhinnam aḥaumadhyamalaṅkṛtam dvitīyaṃ kathitaṃ devi tṛtīyaṃ vamamadhyagam  KubjT ṭhalamadhyāsanāsīnaṃ caturthasvarabheditam bindunā samāyuktam aupaścimavibhūṭitam  KubjT ardhacandrānvitaṃ kṛtvā bindunādayutaṃ kuru pañcapraṇavamuddhāraṃ rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ tava  KubjT mantrāṇāṃ dīpakaṃ devi yathākarmaṇi yojayet vidyāyās tu prasaṅgena pañcapraṇavam uddhṛtam  KubjT sāmprataṃ śṛṇu kalyāṇi vidyāmāhātmyam uttamam sevanāj japahomād vā dhyānāc ca kramaśo bhavet  KubjT ṣaṇmāsāc cotpated devi sat yam etad udāhṛtam kṛtvā sāmrāṭajān doṣān uccārāt kalmaṣāpaham  KubjT devadrohe gurudrohe koṭitriṃśaiḥ sa śudhyati chedane puṣpapattrāṇām āvartāc chudhyate tu saḥ  KubjT sandhyālope kṛte devi trirāvarteṇa śudhyati āhnikacchedasañjāte śatam ekam udīrayet  KubjT laṅghane samayānāṃ ca abhakṣyasya tu bhakṣaṇe avācyavācite devi sahasrāc chuddhir iṣyate  KubjT kākolūkakapotānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ ghātane kṛte sahasrair dvibhiḥ śudhyeta satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  KubjT chāgameṣa tathānyāni mṛgajambūka ṛkṣayoḥ śuddhis trisahasrād devi yathā bhairavamabravīt  KubjT sarpamārjārahantāro dundubhomatsyaghātakaḥ caturbhiś ca sahasrair hi śīghraṃ śuddhim avāpnuyāt  KubjT śvasūkaranakulādi mūṣakaś cātha vāpi vā pañcabhiḥ śuddhir iṣyeta sahasrais tu kulānvaye  KubjT gavāṃ hatvā praśudhyeta daśalakṣais tu saṅkhyayā brāhmaṇas tu yadā devi pramādād ghātito budhaiḥ  KubjT lakṣair viṃśati śudhyeta naktāśī tu jitendriyaḥ bauddhārahantahantā ca dvijād dviguṇa śudhyati  KubjT lākulā mauṣalāś caiva ye cānye lātapāṇayaḥ hatvā śuddhim avāpnoti koṭitrayajapena tu  KubjT guruṃ hatvā pañca koṭyaḥ śudhyate tu pramādataḥ striyo ghātī durācāro daśa koṭyo japet priye  KubjT naktāśī śuddhim āpnoti kṣetrapīṭhān bhramed yadi anyeṣāṃ varṇajātīnām adhamottamamadhyamāḥ  KubjT lakṣais tu bhavate śuddhir dvitricatvārisaṅkhyayā ekād ekona kartavyaṃ varṇāṇāṃ ca krameṇa tu  KubjT nindate yoginīṃ yas tu śivabhaktāṃś ca nindati śāstrāṇi dūṣayed yas tu striyam ākoṭayeti ca  KubjT kroṣanti kanyakā devi sahasrāc chuddhir iṣyate vāmadakṣiṇasiddhānte śivavratadharo hataḥ  KubjT koṭicaturbhir deveśi śudhyate japatatparaḥ yaḥ punas tattvavettā ca ṣoḍhānyāsaviśāradaḥ  KubjT smaraṇāc chuddhir iṣyeta tathyaṃ bhairavamabravīt krodhena tu yadā devi uccaiḥśabdapralāpitam  KubjT trivārāvartayed vidyāṃ śāntim āśu prayacchati kṛte karmaṇi bālānāṃ lūtācipiṭagaṇḍayoḥ  KubjT jvaragrahaviṣādibhyaḥ oṣadhākhyāpanāya ca pañcāvartād viśudhyeta anvayī yas tu śāsane  KubjT yaḥ punaḥ kramavettā ca śuddhāśuddhair na bādhyate deśikaṃ putrakaṃ vāpi sādhakaṃ samayajñakam  KubjT pramādān nindate yas tu daśāvartād viśudhyati aliṃ jugupsayed yas tu phalguṣaṃ vā yadi priye  KubjT ekoccāreṇa śudhyeta annaṃ vā yaj jugupsate kandukaṃ mallakoṣāḍhyā chippakaṃ carmakārakam  KubjT dhvajaṃ sūnākaraṃ vāpi matsyaghātaṃ tu lubdhakam koṅkaṇaṃ cīnabāhlīkaṃ vaṅgālaṃ kāmarūpakam  KubjT māgadhaṃ saindhavaṃ vāpi gujjaraṃ lāṭasaṃjñakam anye pi deśamadhyasthā vanavāsāntyajātayaḥ  KubjT veśyādikramaśaḥ sarve nindanāc chuddhir iṣyate trirāvarteṇa deveśi akāmāt kāmato pi vā  KubjT kāmato dviguṇaṃ devi kartavyaṃ siddhim icchatā trikhaṇḍā yādṛśaṃ proktaṃ prāyaścittaṃ kulānvaye  KubjT dvātriṃśākṣarayā tadvat kartavyaṃ tattvavedibhiḥ ete nirodharūpās tu sādhakānāṃ prakāśitāḥ  KubjT tadarthe kathitā vidyā yena sidhyanti sādhakāḥ śreyārthināṃ mayākhyātā madbhaktāḥ kṛtaniścayāḥ  KubjT anyeṣāṃ na kadācit syāl laulyārthe ye sthitānaghe iyaṃ vidyā samākhyātā upayogād varānane  KubjT sāmprataṃ padabhedas tu yathā yojyas tu bhairavi tathā te kathayiṣyāmi tac chṛṇuṣva samāsataḥ  KubjT yā vidyā kathitā pūrvaṃ nādiphāntakrameṇa tu taccharīragatā varṇāḥ pañcapraṇavabheditāh  KubjT pañcayonyāḥ svarūpeṇa varṇam ekaikasaṅkhyayā bhairavaḥ śabdarāśis tu ādikṣāntakrameṇa tu  KubjT te varṇāḥ pañcapraṇavaiḥ sampuṭec ca pṛthak pṛthak ādikṣāntakrameṇaiva niyojanam udāhṛtam  KubjT dvābhyāṃ tu grathanaṃ kāryaṃ samastasyāpi śobhane sapta varṇān dadec cādau madhye vidyāpadaṃ dadet  KubjT punaḥ sapta padasyānte tasyānte tu padaṃ punaḥ punaḥ saptakam uccārya padaṃ ca tadanantaram  KubjT anena kramayogena nirvāhena tu yojayet kṣāntaṃ vai yāva deveśi tāvad eva niyojayet  KubjT padasaṅkhyā samastasya nirvāhobhayadīpite mālinī dvādaśair bhedaiḥ śabdarāśis tu ṣoḍaśaiḥ  KubjT anena kramaśaḥ sarve varṇāś caiva pṛthak pṛthak calacakravibhāgena padavidyāṃ yadā yajet  KubjT tadā kṣobhaṃ karoty āśu divyādivyetaraṃ priye yonayaḥ pañcadhā yās tu sarvāḥ klidyanti nānyathā  KubjT drāvaṇaṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ mohaṃ jṛmbhaṇaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ tathā sarvān tān kurute devi yadā śaktisamo bhavet  KubjT prasuptabhujagākārā dvādaśānte varānane nābhiṣṭhā tu tathāpy evaṃ draṣṭavyā parameśvari  KubjT dṛśyate dehamadhye tu vyomānte ca parāparā tasyāgre tu tato mantraṃ hutāśakaṇikākṛtim  KubjT uccāreta tato mantraṃ śabdarūpaṃ hṛdi priye śabdānte śaktir uccāryā īṣanmandagamārutā  KubjT padmasūtranibhākārā uccāryā sānunāsikā uccārāntāvasāne tu jñātavyālātacakravat  KubjT tatra madhyagataṃ devi caitanyaṃ mantrasaṃyutam prasphuratkiraṇānekaiḥ koṭiśo dikṣv avasthitaiḥ  KubjT tasyāpy ante tato devi śaktir ādyā manonmanī atītā tu yadā sā vai tadā bindvī udāhṛtā  KubjT bindvante vyāpako devo māyātīto nirāmayaḥ sa śivo bhāvanātīto nirguṇo guṇasambhavaḥ  KubjT adhikārī sarvakārī ca śaktyātīto mahāprabhuḥ anena kramayogena kramaḥ kāryaḥ suniścitaiḥ  KubjT ātmā manaś ca mantraś ca śivaḥ śaktis tathaiva ca ekībhāvagato devi jñātavyaḥ siddhim īhakaiḥ  KubjT tasmāt prāṇasamaṃ jāpyaṃ mantrānte nādagocare nādasyānte tato jñātvā etat smaraṇam ucyate  KubjT smaraṇaṃ śaktir uddiṣṭā yā karoti gamāgamam tasyānte tu parā sūkṣmā sā kalā amṛtātmikā  KubjT layātītā arūpā tu svayaṃvedyāvicārataḥ na tasya lakṣaṇaṃ devi na lakṣo naiva yojanā  KubjT na kṣayo naiva vṛddhiś ca śuklakṛṣṇau na caiva hi na rātrir na dinaṃ caiva na sandhyā ayanaṃ tathā  KubjT viṣuvaṃ naiva deveśi saṅkrāntir naiva vidyate sarvāvasthagatiṃ jñātvā vijñānam upajāyate  KubjT etat kaulikam ākhyātam umāmāheśvaraṃ priye utpateta na sandeho lakṣajāpāc calasya tu  KubjT calā śaktiḥ samākhyātā lakṣaṇena udāhṛtā avarṇā varṇasaṃyogā mālinī sā udāhṛtā  KubjT padabhedagatā hy ekā asaṅkhyātā varānane evaṃ tadgrahamākhyātaḥ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaḥ  KubjT na kasyacin mayākhyātam umāmāheśvaraṃ priye satataṃ japate yas tu yoginīvallabho bhavet  KubjT ṣaṇmāsāc chudhyate devi brahmaghno pi na saṃśayaḥ paśyate virajāṃ śāntāṃ jyotirūpāṃ mahādyutim  KubjT japasya lakṣaṇaṃ devi idānīṃ śṛṇu sāmpratam ekoccāraśatānte tu parāvasthā tu gīyate  KubjT śatabhedaḥ samākhyātas tadguṇo daśa eva tu sahasrabhedam ity uktaṃ lakṣaḥ śataguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  KubjT koṭibhedaḥ śatānāṃ tu lakṣāṇāṃ varavarṇini etaj japavidhānaṃ tu kathitaṃ tava śobhane  KubjT muktakaḥ śatabhedena yuktaṃ śataguṇaṃ śatam calacakravibhāgena lakṣabhedam udāhṛtam  KubjT calacakraṃ yadā devi koṭibhedo varānane bāhyataḥ kathito bhadre adhyātmikam ataḥ śṛṇu  KubjT udbhave śatabhedas tu sahasro viśleṣake viduḥ laye tu lakṣabhedo vai layātīte tu koṭayaḥ  KubjT vāmā jyeṣṭhā tathā raudrī bindvī ca samudāhṛtā icchā jñānī kriyā śāntā krameṇaiva surārcite  KubjT ātmacāragatiṃ jñātvā japaḥ kāryaḥ sadā budhaiḥ anenaivākṣasūtreṇa lakṣalakṣaṇalakṣite  KubjT kartavyo hi japo nityaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradaiḥ bhuvanākhye varārohe śaktyākhye tu tathaiva hi  KubjT cāroccāravibhāgena japaḥ śreṣṭha udāhṛtaḥ mālā pañcāśikā proktā sūtraṃ śaktiḥ śivātmikā  KubjT grathanaṃ kuṇḍalī śaktir layānte merusaṃsthitam etad guptataraṃ kāryam akṣasūtraṃ śivātmakam  KubjT prakaṭaṃ naiva kartavyaṃ na meruṃ laṅghayet kvacit śaṅkhasphaṭikarudrākṣaputrañ jīvakariṣṭakāḥ  KubjT evamādyāḥ smṛtā ye tu maṇimālā varānane na tatra vidyate devo na mantro naiva cetanā  KubjT yatra yatra sthitā mālā na doṣo vidyate priye mantranyāse kṛte devi kila gopyaṃ tu kārayet  KubjT śarīraṃ kutra gopyaṃ tu kārayīta varānane mantranyāse kṛte hy ātmā sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ  KubjT yathā gopyaṃ na yuñjeta tadvac caivākṣamālikā akṣaṃ cendriyam ity uktaṃ sūtraṃ kuṇḍalinī smṛtā  KubjT lakṣaṃ tu sā parā sūkṣmā kalā hy amṛtavāhinī saṃyogakāriṇī vyomni tena sūtreti kīrtitā  KubjT saṅkhyāgrahaṇakāryeṣu sā coktā akṣamālikā śaṅkhādyās tu varārohe japakarmaṇi śasyate  KubjT śaṅkhajaṃ tu śriyākāmaḥ sphāṭikaṃ muktihetave padmākṣā padmajā proktā śriyāpuṣṭikarā priye  KubjT rudrākṣaiḥ siddhim āpnoti yac cānyaṃ khecarīpadam jīvakā sarvadā jñeyā gopucchāgrathitānaghe  KubjT vidrumā vaśyakāryeṣu mauktikā sarvakāmadā anyāni tu smṛtā ye vai ratnajā parameśvari  KubjT sarvadā te samuddiṣṭā nātra kāryavicāraṇāt riṣṭakākṣāsthijā mālā abhicāre praśasyate  KubjT nāgavaṅgas tathā lohā miśrāś cānye pi ye smṛtāḥ māraṇe tāṃ praśasyeta stambhane mohane tathā  KubjT kampane dhvaṃsane devi kartavyā cābhicārake evam anye pi ye proktās teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā tu śaṅkhajā  KubjT praśastā sarvakāryeṣu japakarmaṇi śasyate śaṅkhāvartā tu yā nāḍī śikhānte tu vyavasthitā  KubjT tena śaṅkhamayaṃ proktam akṣasūtraṃ surādhipe sphuṭate mastake yā sā dvidhā caiva visarpiṇī  KubjT sphāṭikaṃ tena coddiṣṭaṃ guruvaktre pratiṣṭhitam raudrībhāvaḥ smṛto rudras tālvagre ca vyavasthitaḥ  KubjT śabdasparśaraso rūpaṃ gandhatanmātrasaṃyutam vikāritve pravarteta nirodhāl lakṣam eva ca  KubjT tena rudrākṣamālāyā japaḥ śreṣṭha udāhṛtaḥ putravad udare kṛtvā prasuptāmṛtakuṇḍalī  KubjT tayā nīyaty asau jīva adhaś cordhvena bhāvini putrañjīvakasaṃjñā tu tenaiṣā samudāhṛtā  KubjT ariṣṭāni anekāni sukhaduḥkhātmikāni tu bhuñjate satataṃ devi arjitaṃ yat purā dhanam  KubjT ariṣṭākhyā smṛtā mālā aprameyā bhavāntare hṛtpadme saṃsthitā nityam akṣarāṇāṃ prabodhikā  KubjT padmākṣamālā sā proktā śāstre śāstre varānane evamādyāḥ smṛtā ye tu paryāyā akṣamālayā  KubjT te sarve ātmanaś caiva kathitāś ca kuleśvari akṣasūtravidhiḥ khyātaḥ samyak kaulikavedinām  KubjT sāmprataṃ nyāsam ākhyāmi śṛṇu tattvena śobhane svābhāvikaṃ calaṃ dīptaṃ sthiraṃ dravanabhoyutam  KubjT nyāsamātraṃ samākhyātaṃ ṣoḍhādvādaśabhedataḥ ṣoḍhā śaktiḥ samākhyātā parā caivākṣarā śubhā  KubjT kuṇḍalī nābhideśasthā parā sā vyomarūpiṇī ekā eva parā sūkṣmā akṣayā tejarūpiṇī  KubjT jñātavyā sā parā devī ṣaḍvarṇarahitā kalā brahmasthānagatā sūkṣmā svābhāvikam udāhṛtā  KubjT viṣṇusthāne calā proktā dīptā rudrapade smṛtā īśvare sthirasaṃjñā tu sadākhye dravasambhavā  KubjT śaktisthā vyomarūpā tu jñātavyā tattvavedibhiḥ aṇimādiguṇādhārā ṣaḍguṇā guṇabodhanī  KubjT vyāpinī vyomarūpā ca anantānāthanāśritā saṃyoktrī ca viyoktrī ca sadbhāvaguṇasaṃsthitā  KubjT ekā eva parā śaktiḥ saṃsthitā kṛtyabhedataḥ kṛtyabhedena bhedo syā na bhedaḥ paramārthataḥ  KubjT evaṃ nyāse kṛte devi antaraṅge pravartate bahiraṅge varṇarūpā ca ekā caiva anekadhā  KubjT ṣoḍhādvādaśabhedena nyāsaḥ prokto gamāgame  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate bṛhatsamayoddhāraḥ śabdarāśimālinītadgrahavyāptinirṇayo nāma pañcamaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrīkubjikā uvācajapasya lakṣaṇaṃ deva pūrvaṃ hi kathitaṃ tvayā ekoccāraśataṃ jñeyaṃ sahasraṃ lakṣam eva ca  KubjT koṭayas tu tathā śambho pṛthaglakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ na me jñātaṃ pramāṇaṃ tu japasya suranāyaka  KubjT tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi mandabuddhyālpacetasā  KubjT śrībhairava uvācayā sā kuṇḍalinī śaktis cidrūpā ca parā kalā ādyā śaktir maheśasya aṇumātrā hṛdi sthitā  KubjT sā aṇuḥ  kathitā tantre dve aṇū truṭim āśritā truṭibhūtā tu sā devī japtavyā tu parāparā  KubjT varṇahīnā parā proktā aparā varṇarūpiṇī evaṃ jñātvā varārohe japaḥ kāryaḥ sadā budhaiḥ  KubjT truṭirūpā tu sā devī tadādhāre vyavasthitā kalate prāṇagā nityaṃ daśasthāne hy anukramāt  KubjT brahmā viṣṇus tathā rudra īśvaro tha sadāśivaḥ kuṇḍalī vyāpinī caiva praśāntā viṣuvat tathā  KubjT śaktisthānaṃ tu deveśi ete sthānā daśa smṛtāḥ yeṣāṃ sañcarate devaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇaḥ  KubjT ūrdhve vā yadi vā tiryak svasthāne vā sureśvari prasphureta kalair yuktā daśabhis tu mahābalaiḥ  KubjT daśadhā kalanaṃ tena kathitaṃ tava śobhane prayatnena kṛtoccāraṃ yāvac chaktir layaṃ gatā  KubjT tāvad devi śataṃ proktaṃ varṇoccāre na saṃśayaḥ svābhāvikam anuccārya sūkṣmādhāro jagatpatiḥ  KubjT śatadhā kalanaṃ tasya truṭirūpasya yoginaḥ sahasraṃ tu samuddiṣṭaṃ daśadhā parameśvari  KubjT ubhayasya parityāgād kalādhāraḥ sadāśivaḥ dṛkkriyājñānanirmuktaḥ kalate ca sahasradhā  KubjT lakṣabhedaḥ samuddiṣṭa iti śāstre na saṃśayaḥ japo hy evaṃ samuddiṣṭo yogināṃ tattvavedinām  KubjT lakṣātīto manātīto nirmuktas tattvabandhanaiḥ unmanatve sadā līno aṇurūpo nakiñcanaḥ  KubjT sattāmātrasthito dehī guṇānāṃ pratibodhakaḥ viṣayabhāvanirmuktaḥ kalate lakṣadhā priye  KubjT koṭis tu bhavate hy evaṃ jñātavyaṃ mantravādibhiḥ soccāropāṃśubhūtas tu mānaso manavarjitaḥ  KubjT japaḥ pūrvaṃ samākhyātaḥ śāstre śāstre surārcite saśabdoccārayogena śuddhyarthe kathitaṃ sphuṭam  KubjT siddhyarthe pāṃśur uddiṣṭaḥ svapravṛtto hṛdi sthitaḥ mānaso yogahetvarthe ubhayatra vivarjitaḥ  KubjT manātīto bhaved devi mokṣadas tu na saṃśayaḥ evaṃ devi samākhyāto japaḥ prāṇasamas tava  KubjT japaḥ prāṇasamaḥ kāryo dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalārthinām avarṇā varṇasaṃyogā mayā te samudāhṛtā  KubjT nirālambe mahāśūnye yat tejam upajāyate tadgarbhe abhyasen nityaṃ bhāgyahīno pi sidhyati  KubjT yogamūlī viśuddhī ca sārṇave sā ca ekatā ekatra saṃsthitānandaṃ kularatnaṃ tridhā priye  KubjT śrīkubjikā uvācamudrā tu sūcitā nātha na me jñātā mahāprabho tan mamācakṣva deveśi yena bhrāntir vinaśyati  KubjT śrībhairava uvācapātālordhvagataṃ yac ca śṛṅgāṭapuramadhyagam golākāraṃ tato devi randhrasyordhvagataṃ priye  KubjT cakradvayam idaṃ proktaṃ prādhānyena vyavasthitam vedhaghaṭṭanirodhaṃ ca uccārākṛṣṭikārakam  KubjT stobhastambhanam āveśo gamaṃ caivātra suvrate etadvirahito mantrī hāsyatāṃ yāti niścitam  KubjT anena jñātamātreṇa pratyayān kurute bahūn vṛttirājā varārohe niveśya cakramadhyataḥ  KubjT vṛttihīnas tatas tatra kāvyakartā na saṃśayaḥ cakramadhye ca sañcintya suśuklāṃ ca parāparām  KubjT pustakavyagrahastāṃ ca jñānamudrādharāṃ tathā sphāṭikenākṣasūtreṇa sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām  KubjT sragdāmalambitagalāṃ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitām dvibāhurekavadanāṃ candrakoṭisamaprabhām  KubjT udgirantī ṃ  mahaughena śāstrakoṭīr anekaśaḥ evaṃ dhyānasamāviṣṭaḥ sākṣād vāgīśvaro bhavet  KubjT saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ caiva vedasiddhāntagahvaram granthataś cārthataś caiva udgiren nātra saṃśayaḥ  KubjT pīṭhamadhyagatābhyāsāt pīṭhadvāre thavā priye sampradāyam idaṃ kaulaṃ śāktaṃ śaktipadānugam  KubjT mātrāyogena deveśi mudrābandhaṃ tu kārayet sā mātrā gīyate cātra uccāravaśavartinī  KubjT uccaraṃ sahajaṃ devi dehamadhye vyavasthitam śatasaṅkhyāpramāṇena yāvad uccarate parām  KubjT tāvad āviṣṭadehas tu śāstrārthaṃ vadate sudhīḥ nityārūpeṇa saivātra dhyāyed raktasamaprabhām  KubjT lākṣālaktakasaṅkāśāṃ caturvaktrāṃ caturbhujām mūrtitrayasamopetāṃ tribhir bhedair vyavasthitām  KubjT tristhāṃ trimārgagāṃ devīṃ trināḍīsamatāṃ gatām nityaklinnāṃ ca deveśi tathā caiva madadravām  KubjT devyārūpadharāṃ sarvām ekavaktrāṃ dvibāhukām pāśāṅkuśadharāṃ sarvāṃ madavibhrāntalocanām  KubjT yauvanasthāṃ madonmattāṃ madirānandananditām smared devyāḥ svarūpaṃ tu tatprayogavyavasthayā  KubjT taḍitsahasrabandhūka dāḍimīkusumadyutim pañcaśṛṅgāṭakādhārāṃ sā parā pararūpiṇī  KubjT mahāyogavilāsā tu śivādyavanigocaram vyāpayitvā sthitā devī ravinakṣatramaṇḍalam  KubjT śṛṅgāṭakaṃ cordhvamukhaṃ tiryagrekhāgramūlagam śikhordhvakuṇḍalākāraṃ kāmaśaktiradhisthitam  KubjT pañcaśṛṅgāṭakāsīnaṃ sthitaṃ tatra varānane devyārūpadharaṃ cakraṃ dhyāyed evaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  KubjT eṣa bandhas tu mudrāyāḥ kathitas te kuleśvari tritattvena tu mantreṇa vakṣyamānena kārayet  KubjT drāvaṇaṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ caiva ākarṣavaśam eva ca pūjāvidhānaṃ deveśi devyāyā vīravandite  KubjT śrīkubjikā uvācatriśikhā padmamudrā ca yonimudrā viśeṣataḥ tāsāṃ lakṣaṇam ākhyāhi yathāvat sphuṭato vada  KubjT śrībhairava uvācamudrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ devi kathayāmi samāsataḥ hastābhyāṃ kārayed ādau sampuṭaṃ cordhvadiṅmukham  KubjT aṅgulyā grathayet sarvāḥ saṃśliṣṭam ubhayeṣv api tarjanyānāmikau kuñcya saṃśliṣṭau madhyasaṃsthitau  KubjT tābhyāṃ mūle mukhaṃ kāryaṃ tarjanyāyā varānane saṃśliṣṭau sammukhau dvau tu madhyamau ūrdhvadiṅmukhau  KubjT saṃyogena varārohe aṅguṣṭhau ca kaniṣṭhakau tādṛśīva hi kartavyā triśikhā tu vidhīyate  KubjT karābhyāṃ sampuṭaṃ kāryaṃ maṇibandhau tu saṃhatau agrāṅgulyā prasāryeta aṅguṣṭhau madhyasaṃsthitau  KubjT padmamudrā samākhyātā yonimudrām ataḥ śṛṇu hastābhyāṃ sampuṭaṃ kāryaṃ kaniṣṭhā madhya yojayet  KubjT puṭākārau karau kṛtvā aṅguṣṭhau madhyasaṃsthitau niḥsṛtā vāmahastasya aṅgulyā tu kanīyasī  KubjT yonimudrā smṛtā bhadre sarveṣāṃ kṣobhakārikā etā mudrāḥ samākhyātā dhyānapūjāvisarjane  KubjT sāmprataṃ khecarīṇāṃ tu yathā mudrā khagādhipe kathayāmi samāsena tvatprītyā khagagāminī  KubjT anāmā karṇike yojyā ṣoḍaśāraṃ tu pīḍayet pīḍanād ṛjutāṃ yāti khagamārge tu bhāvini  KubjT phādināntagate lakṣe khagatiś ca na saṃśayaḥ ṣaṭpattraṃ mūrdhnitaḥ kṛtvā tarjanyāgre tu yojayet  KubjT śūnye śūnyamano bhūtvā sampīḍyeta parasparam ṣaṭpattraṃ tu vikāśyeta udānapreritena tu  KubjT bhāvayen nādiphāntaṃ tu khagatīti na saṃśayaḥ dvādaśārordhvanālena lambikānte niveśayet  KubjT bhedanaṃ kuñcitenaiva cārgalaṃ kūrmasaṃyutam bhāvayen nādiphāntaṃ tu khagatiṃ vīravandite  KubjT padmamudrā tridhā proktā yonimudrām ataḥ śṛṇu yoniṃ yonau samākramya mudgareṇa tu bhedanam  KubjT visargadvayasaṃyogāt khagagāmī bhaved dhruvam amṛtākhyā parā yonir bhāvayen mastakopari  KubjT ākramya gandhamārgaṃ tu yojanā nādiphāntagā khagatir bhavatedevaṃ yonimārge vicakṣaṇaḥ  KubjT uccārya vāmaśaktiṃ tu sandhayed granthimadhyataḥ vikṣepam ūrdhvataḥ kṛtvā pare yonau tu bhāvanā  KubjT anena khagagāmitvaṃ bhavate tu na saṃśayaḥ yonimudrā samākhyātā tribhedā parikīrtitā  KubjT triśikhālakṣaṇaṃ devi kathyamānaṃ nibodhata karābhyāṃ caiva tarjanyāṃ pīḍayet tat prayatnataḥ  KubjT brahmanāḍyā dvirabhyāsād āsanaṃ mandarasya tu triśikhā nāma mudreyam arpaṇaṃ khagamārgayoḥ  KubjT golakaṃ śūnyamārgasthaṃ pathatrayagataṃ priye kṣepaṇaṃ bindukoṭyūrdhvam avanīṃ kramya pādayoḥ  KubjT guhye niveśya mantrajñas triśikhaṃ khecaraṃ priye anena khagagāmī sau bhavate sādhakottamaḥ  KubjT karaṇaṃ cordhvamūlaṃ syād bandhayet khagamaṇḍalam ākramya pañcamaṃ tatra karābhyāṃ caiva śūlini  KubjT jānukau kurpare yojya vikṣepo guhyamadhyataḥ vedhanaṃ brahmarandhrasya kathitaṃ tu tapodhane  KubjT khagamārgagatis tv evaṃ bhavate tu sulocane eṣā mudrā samākhyātā navabhedair vyavasthitā  KubjT mudrā śaktir iti khyātā mudritaṃ drāvayiṣyati tena mudrā samākhyātā kathitā parameśvari  KubjT mudritaṃ gopitaṃ proktaṃ cicchaktyā yā parāparā na jñāyate varārohe sā tu mudrā udāhṛtā  KubjT ajñānamalarūpeṇa yāvad baddhaḥ sa pudgalaḥ na jānāti parātmānaṃ tāvan māyā pravartate  KubjT bhinne tamasi caikatvaṃ yadā paśyati mānavaḥ tadā sā tu parā proktā bandhamokṣakarī priye  KubjT ekā sā paramā śaktiḥ saṃsthitā tu śivecchayā mocayanti grahādibhyaḥ pāśaughān drāvayanti ca  KubjT mocanād drāvaṇād yasmān mudrākhyāḥ śaktayaḥ smṛtāḥ khagatir hy ūrdhvabhāvena khagamārgeṇa nityaśaḥ  KubjT carate sarvajantūnāṃ khecarī tena sā smṛtā paratv ekā tu sā jñeyā punaś caiva tridhā smṛtā  KubjT icchā jñānī kriyā sā tu varṇarūpam upāgatā pañcāśabhedabhinnā sā ekā evamudāhṛtā  KubjT aṅgāvayavasampūrṇā mālayitvā jagat sthitā nādiphāntasvarūpeṇa tena sā mālinī smṛtā  KubjT sapta koṭyas tu mantrāṇām aprameyās tu yāḥ smṛtāḥ svatantrasthās tu tāḥ sarvā mudritāḥ parameśvari  KubjT tena mudrā samākhyātā sadyaḥpratyayakārikā avayave mātṛrūpā tu svaiḥ svair aṃśair vyavasthitā  KubjT brahmāṃśā caiva rudrāṃśā kaumāryāṃśā varānane vaiṣṇavyā caiva yāmyāṃśā aindryāṃśā ca tathānaghe  KubjT yogeśvaryā ca yogāṃśā yogayogīśanāyikā ete hy aṃśāḥ smṛtāḥ sapta punaḥ saptasu saptasu  KubjT brahmāṇyāḥ saptamuddiṣṭāḥ sapta māheśvarī punaḥ kaumāryāḥ saptamuddiṣṭā vaiṣṇavyāḥ sapta eva ca  KubjT vārāhī saptamuddiṣṭā aindrāṇyāḥ sapta eva tu cāmuṇḍā saptamuddiṣṭā evaṃ vai sapta saptasu  KubjT pañcāśaikona vai devyā bhuvanāvalisaṃsthitāḥ atra bhedair anekaiś ca saṃsthitā bhuvanāvaliḥ  KubjT tasya dehagatā romāḥ koṭyas trīṇi prakīrtitāḥ lakṣāṇi caiva pañcāśad romāṇāṃ tu tadudbhavā  KubjT ekaikaromakūpeṣu yoginyaḥ koṭisaṃsthitāḥ trikoṭikoṭikoṭīnāṃ koṭayas tu anekadhā  KubjT yathā cāmbaraparyantā pṛthivyādiṣu sambhavāḥ aṇavas tv apramāṇās tu tattve tattve tv anekadhā  KubjT sūkṣmarūpās tathā rudrā eṣāṃ saṅkhyā na vidyate vyāpitaṃ tu samastaṃ hi rudraiḥ sūkṣmataraiḥ priye  KubjT evaṃ mudrā samākhyātā vyāpayitvāprameyataḥ ekā eva parā mudrā yasyedaṃ tiṣṭhate jagat  KubjT yaṃ yaṃ spṛśati sā hy aṅgaṃ sā sā mudrā vidhīyate nṛtyaṃ valgaṃ tathā hāsyaṃ rodanaṃ sphoṭam eva ca  KubjT yad vikāraṃ prakurvanti tat sarvaṃ mudrasaṃjñakam aṅgulyā aṅganā proktā aṅge carati nityaśaḥ  KubjT aṅgulyā tena coddiṣṭā mudrābandhe varānane kaṃ śarīram iti khyātaṃ nyastā tasmin pravartate  KubjT helāgamanamārgeṇa tena nāmā kanīyasī anāmā nāmarahitā koṭibhedair vyavasthitā  KubjT nāmaṃ na śakyate vaktum anāmā tena gīyate madhye pravartate nit yam āśrayā pudgalasya tu  KubjT tatrādhārād vrajed ūrdhvaṃ punarāgamanaṃ priye madhyamā nāma tenātra kathitā mantravādinām  KubjT tarjanaṃ kurute nityaṃ saṃyojanaviyojanam tarjayantī mahāmohaṃ pāśajālam anantakam  KubjT tarjanī tena sā proktā mudrā sarveṣu cottamā aṅguṣṭhaś caughabhūtā tu pravāhe satataṃ priye  KubjT uccāreṇa pravarteta aṅguṣṭhas tena sa smṛtaḥ ahamūrdhvagatiḥ proktaḥ stau ti rātrī nigadyate  KubjT hastau tena samākhyātau vāmadakṣiṇa ucyate vāme sṛṣṭir iti proktā saṃhāraṃ dakṣiṇe viduḥ  KubjT savyāsavyagatau tena kathitau vīranāyike vāmāvyāptaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ saṃhārāntaṃ tadā priye  KubjT saṃyogena varārohe ātmā kuṇḍalinī smṛtā iyaṃ sā paramā yonir yonīnām uttamā priye  KubjT yo jānāti varārohe śaktir ādyā manonmanī tena jñātaṃ jagat sarvaṃ varṇāvarṇavivarjitam  KubjT sā mudrā tu samākhyātā viśvavyāptikarī parā dvau bindū cūlike dve tu visargaśaktisampuṭam  KubjT tadūrdhvam iha nādāntaṃ vibhvī śūnyam udāhṛtam janmasthānāt samudyantī yāvat tadbhavamaṇḍalam  KubjT sṛṣṭisaṃhārayogena meḍhramādhāramadhyagam evaṃ mudrā samākhyātā vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ  KubjT kim anyat pṛcchase devi tat sarvaṃ kathayāmy aham  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate japamudrānirṇayo nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrīkubjikā uvācayā sā devī deva Edparā yoniḥ samayā kubjinī parā tām ācakṣva prayatnena saṃsphuṭaṃ vyāptilakṣaṇam  KubjT śrībhairava uvācaśṛṇu devi yathātathyaṃ devyā māhātmyam uttamam kārye vātha akārye vā uktānukteṣu vastuṣu  KubjT kubjīśānīṃ japed yas tu tasya pāpaṃ na vidyate yaḥ punaḥ śuddhabhāvātmā samayākhyāṃ maheśvarīm  KubjT japet tasya pa tad vastu yan na sidhyati bhūtale etat paramasamayaṃ devītantre prakīrtitam  KubjT na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi yasmāt sarvaṃ prapadyate tantre tantre tu samayā kathitānekadhā mayā  KubjT anyakalpopacāreṣu niruddhā tatra śāsane eṣā sā samayā devi atra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  KubjT catuṣpīṭheṣu samayās te tra sarve vinirgatāḥ eṣā rājeśvarī devī samayācāranirgatā  KubjT nirācāreṇa yogena sidhyate hy avicārataḥ pañcavyāptam ataḥ sarvaṃ sarvavyāptyantasaṃsthitam  KubjT asyoccāraṇamātreṇa tan nāsti yan na sādhayet kampate bhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ suraḍāmaram  KubjT samayākhyaṃ japantasya kṣubhyate sacarācaram vāmadakṣiṇatantreṣu sāmānyā samayā parā  KubjT tasyā devyāḥ prabhāvo yaṃ yā pañcāśapadātmikā siddhamārge nyathā devi dvātriṃśaguṇalakṣitā  KubjT kubjikā nāma vikhyātā samayasthā kuleśvarī yatra viśveśvaraṃ sarvaṃ samayādyaṃ vinirgatam  KubjT mantramudrāgaṇo hy atra vidyāmaṇḍalakādikam yasyāḥ kamalinī devī hṛdisthā sampravartate  KubjT yayā sṛṣṭam idaṃ sarvam ābrahmastambhagocaram kuladīpā śirasthāsyāḥ ṣaḍvidhādhvaprabodhikā  KubjT barbarākhyā śikhā hy asyās tritattvordhvavyavasthitā mudrādhāragatā devī bahurūpātra nirgatā  KubjT chādayantī samastāṃ tu śabdarāśiṃ tu mālinī kavacaṃ yasyā mahādevyā mantramāyātmakaṃ mahat  KubjT kiṇkiṇiṃ taṃ pracaṇḍograṃ tejodedīpyavarcasam jñeyaṃ vṛddhopamaṃ netraṃ tattvārthaguṇasaṅkulam  KubjT saṃvartādiśivāntasthaṃ ṣaḍasraṃ piṅgalocanam tad astraṃ koṅkaṇeśānyā yena vyāptaṃ ṣaḍadhvaram  KubjT śrīkubjikā uvācakathaṃ tu kubjikā nātha vada mantrapadānvitam sarvajñā sarvadā devī lakṣaṇena samanvitā  KubjT uvāca bhairavo hy evaṃ kubjikāṃ śṛṇu kubjike kiṃ tu tvayā na vaktavyā yāvan nādeśitaḥ śiśuḥ  KubjT ccevīti padaṃ prathamaṃ ṇiki ṇiki dvitīyakam chīṃ chāṃ padaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu khimurāghoa caturthakam  KubjT me na ṇa ña ṅa pañcamaṃ hrauṃ hrīṃ hrāṃ ṣaṣṭhamaṃ padam yaikābjikuśrī saptamaṃ tivagabha mona aṣṭamam  KubjT vilomena padāny aṣṭau dvātriṃśākṣaramālikā pañcapraṇavamādyantā viyuktā lakṣaṇādhikā  KubjT ādikūṭāvasāne tu catvāriṃśad dhi mālinī vilomenoddhared devīṃ guruvaktropadeśataḥ  KubjT rephasaham idaṃ kūṭaṃ vidyāsaptamakaṃ padam śrīlope sanniyoktavyaṃ jīvitaṃ kubjike mama  KubjT svamanīṣikāto nyathā sa vidviṣṭo marīcibhiḥ yasmād bhāṇḍāram ity evaṃ sarvasvaṃ yoginīkule  KubjT atha cet sarvapīṭheṣu māteyaṃ samayātmikā asyāḥ smaraṇamātreṇa vihvalaṃ tu jagattrayam  KubjT bhavate nātra sandeha iti mātā surakṣitā hṛdayādyastraparyantam ekoccāreṇa suvrate  KubjT siddhamārgaṃ yathā brūmi vilomena vilomataḥ  KubjT yastrāa yaivvāṇāṅkako ccevi ṇiki ṇiki yayātratrane yaikārintāhama chīṃ chāṃ yacāvaka yaipārūhuba khimurāghoa me na ṇa ña ṅa yaikhāśi kheśirarbaba hrauṃ hrīṃ hrāṃ seraśi yaipādīlaku yaikābjikuśrī yayādahṛ yailāmatkahṛ tivagabha mona  KubjT pañcadaśākṣaraṃ hṛdayaṃ śiraś caiva trayodaśa ekādaśākṣarā śikhā viṃśadekona kavacam  KubjT netraṃ trayodaśaiḥ proktam astraṃ caiva caturdaśam pañcapraṇavamādyantā yathā vidyā tathā kuru  KubjT etat kaulikabhāṣāyāṃ kathitaṃ tu sapratyayam saṃsphuṭaṃ guruvaktrasthaṃ vilomasthaṃ na sidhyati  KubjT kaulikedaṃ samākhyātaṃ siddhamārgasudurlabham ccevi ti prathamaṃ padaṃ ṇiki ṇiki dvitīyakam  KubjT chīṃ chāṃ caiva tṛtīyaṃ syāt hrauṃ hrīṃ hrāṃ rdhvekhośitri caturthakam hreṃ me na ṇa ña ṅa pañcamaṃ khimurāghoaśrī ṣaṣṭham  KubjT yaikābjiku mona hrīṃ saptamam raphasaha eaṃ kūṭam aiṃ vilomena cāṣṭamam  KubjT dvātriṃśadakṣarā devī niyuktā guṇaśālinī ādikūṭakrameṇaiva vilomenoddhṛtā iyam  KubjT guruvaktropadeśena saṃsphuṭaṃ kathitaṃ tava  KubjT strama vvāṇāṅkako ccevi traṃne nijiteśvavi ṇiki ṇiki caṃvaka keghvila chīṃ chāṃ yaikhāśi kerintāhama hrauṃ hrīṃ hrāṃ me na ṇa ña ṅa seraśi rarbaba khimurāghoaśrī yaṃdahṛ yaikābjikulamaka mona hrīṃ hsphreṃ aiṃ  KubjT sarvasādhāraṇaṃ kaulaṃ brūmi anyopadeśataḥ pañcamaṃ tu padādisthaṃ hṛdayaṃ ca daśākṣaram  KubjT śiram aṣṭākṣaraṃ viddhi dvādaśārdhaṃ śikhā smṛtā dvisaptakaṃ ca kavacaṃ netraṃ saptākṣaraṃ śubham  KubjT astraṃ navākṣaraṃ proktaṃ jātayaś ca pṛthak pṛthak kavacāntaṃ caturvaktraṃ pañcamaṃ tu tadagrataḥ  KubjT paripāṭis tu vaktrāṇām ūrdhvavaktrāditaḥ kramāt eṣā sā samayā devī kulamārge vyavasthitā  KubjT sakalasthā tu sācārā aśeṣārthaviśodhikā kaulabhāṣoditā yā tu sā tu siddhā kulānvaye  KubjT aśeṣārthapradātārā anekārthaprabodhikā yānty anena tu dehena khecaratvaṃ tadāśritāḥ  KubjT akṣarākṣarasantānaṃ yojayellakṣasaṅkhyayā kubjīśaguṇatulyo sau hartā kartā svayaṃ prabhuḥ  KubjT khecarīṇāṃ padaṃ so hi paśyate hy avicārataḥ nirācāreṇa yogena cintayantaḥ kuleśvarīm  KubjT atha sāmānyarūpeṇa tadā bhūcaratāṃ vrajet kupitaḥ pātayec chailān śoṣayej jaladhīśvarān  KubjT sphoṭayec chailavṛkṣāṃś ca taddhyānaguṇam āśritaḥ bhūcarīṇāṃ patitvaṃ ca kṣudrakarmopajīvinām  KubjT kurute vividhāścaryaṃ pūjyate sa śivo yathā yatra tiṣṭhaty asau deśe tatra vighnaṃ palāyate  KubjT kubjikāyāś ca yā dūtī kālikā nāma viśrutā kālikākhye mahātantre svatantrā sā udaḥrtā  KubjT śṛṇuṣvekamanā bhadre jñānavijñānadāyinī sarvasiddhikarī devī sarvakāryaprasādhanī  KubjT vyāghrasiṃhagajavyāla bhūtavetālaśatravaḥ smaraṇān nāśam āyānti vighnasaṅghāni yāni ca  KubjT praśnakāle parīkṣeta kumāry āveśapūrvikā śubhāśubhaṃ vadaty āśu yad bhūtaṃ yad bhaviṣyati  KubjT asyoddhāraṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ aḥkhamadhyagataṃ gṛhya jhapūrveṇa samanvitam  KubjT prathamam uddhṛtaṃ bījaṃ dvitīyaṃ ṇahasandhigam bheditaṃ tu ñapūrveṇa etad varṇadvayaṃ punaḥ  KubjT āsarandhragataṃ gṛhya yasamadhyagataṃ punaḥ dvitīyena tu sambhinnaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai bījam uttamam  KubjT prathamaṃ saptamaṃ jñeyaṃ dvitīyasya dvitīyakam aṣṭamam uddhṛtam bījaṃ navamaṃ bhañamadhyagam  KubjT ñauttarasamāyuktaṃ śūnyamastakabhūṣitam maṣamadhyagataṃ gṛhya daśamaṃ kevalaṃ priye  KubjT ṣavamadhyagatoddhṛtya aupūrveṇa tu bheditam ekādaśākṣaraṃ proktam aiṭhamadhyagataṃ dadet  KubjT ñapūrveṇa tu sambhinnaṃ daśadvitayam uttamam evarandhragataṃ gṛhya kevalaṃ tridaśaṃ punaḥ  KubjT jasamadhyagataṃ gṛhya aiaumadhyena āhatam caturdaśoddhṛtaṃ bījam achasandhigataṃ punaḥ  KubjT kevalaṃ kathitaṃ bījaṃ daśapañcākṣaraṃ priye padhamadhyagataṃ gṛhya ñapūrveṇa tu bheditam  KubjT ṣoḍaśam uddhṛtaṃ bījaṃ sayamadhyagataṃ dadet laṭhamadhyāsanāsīnaṃ jhapūrveṇa tu bheditam  KubjT nādabindukalākrāntaṃ daśasaptakam uddhṛtam vamamadhyagatoddhṛtya ṭaṇamadhyāsane sthitam  KubjT ṭapūrveṇa tu sambhinnaṃ śūnyayuktaṃ daśāṣṭamam vahniyuktaṃ mahāprāṇam aṃpūrveṇa tu bheditam  KubjT caturdaśasvarākrāntaṃ bindunādasaśaktigam viṃśamaṃ nyūnam ekena uddhṛtaṃ bījam uttamam  KubjT yaḍhamadhyagataṃ gṛhya kevalaṃ viṃśamaṃ bhavet khapūrvavarṇam uddhṛtya thapūrvāsanasaṃsthitam  KubjT viṃśam ekādhikaṃ bhadre aḥkhamadhyagataṃ punaḥ ṝpūrvāsanam ārūḍhaṃ dvāviṃśatim udāhṛtam  KubjT dacarandhragatoddhṛtya tapūrvāsanasaṃsthitam viṃśatritayam ākhyātaṃ yajamadhyagataṃ punaḥ  KubjT pañcamasvarasaṃyuktaṃ caturviṃśatimaṃ punaḥ gapūrvaṃ tu samuddhṛtya caturthasvarasaṃyutam  KubjT pañcaviṃśa samākhyātam oṣamadhyagataṃ punaḥ aipūrveṇa tu sambhinnaṃ ṣaḍviṃśakam udāhṛtam  KubjT satamadhyagataṃ cānyaṃ ṭapareṇa samāhatam saptāviṃśatimaṃ bhadre āsamadhyagataṃ punaḥ  KubjT jhapūrveṇa samāyuktam aṣṭāviṃśa tu pārvati punar evaṃ daded devi triṃśatyūnaṃ sabindukam  KubjT ghanamadhyagataṃ gṛhya kevalaṃ triṃśamaṃ bhavet dhaharandhragataṃ devi vāyvāsanasamanvitam  KubjT triṃśam ekādhikaṃ proktaṃ kaṣamadhyagataṃ punaḥ thaṇamadhyāsanārūḍhaṃ pañcamasvarayojitam  KubjT dvātriṃśamaṃ samākhyātaṃ kevalaṃ vaṣamadhyagam trayastriṃśa samuddiṣṭaṃ ṇathamadhyagataṃ punaḥ  KubjT vahninā dīpitaṃ kṛtvā triṃśamaṃ caturādhikam satarandhragataṃ bījaṃ kevalaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃyutam  KubjT pañcatriṃśa smṛtā varṇāḥ pañcapraṇavasampuṭāḥ yojitavyā mahāvidyā kālikā siddhikāṅkṣiṇā  KubjT adṛśīkaraṇe hy eṣā sarvasampadadāyinī na deyā duṣṭabuddhīnāṃ devīdūtyā mahābalā  KubjT dūtī tu kathitā hy evaṃ mudrābandham ataḥ śṛṇu padmāsanasthito yogī samakāya ṛjuḥśiraḥ  KubjT recya vāyuṃ svakād dehāt punar ākṛṣya dhārayet hṛdaye yaḥ sthito granthis tasya nābhau kṣipen manaḥ  KubjT mantraṃ caiva tathātmānam ekīkṛtya trayaṃ budhaḥ daṇḍākāraṃ nayettāvad yāvad brahmabilāntagam  KubjT tatsthānāt prerayet tūrṇaṃ mahāyānena sundari karābhyāṃ caiva tarjanyāṃ pīḍayeta punaḥ punaḥ  KubjT lalanāghaṇṭike yojya pañcamaṃ sthānam ākramet ākramed guhyacakraṃ tu karaṇaṃ cordhvamūlakam  KubjT lagne granthitrayaṃ devi khagatir nātra saṃśayaḥ aṅgaṣaṭkaṃ śṛṇuṣvedaṃ kubjikāyāḥ kuleśvari  KubjT hṛdayena tu devyāyāḥ kṣobhayec cāsurīgaṇam navalakṣakṛte jāpye rājikālavaṇe hute  KubjT rājarājeśvarāṇāṃ tu martyaloke thavā patiḥ sāmānyajapahomena sadyaḥsampadadāyinaḥ  KubjT strījanaṃ kṣobhayet sarvaṃ bālavṛddhayuvān paśūn śiro dhiṣṭhitayogena bhūtavetālarākṣasān  KubjT yakṣiṇīyakṣakanyāś ca piśācīnāṃ ca sādhanam kurute vividhāścaryaṃ phalapuṣpādikarṣaṇam  KubjT yakṣiṇyākarṣaṇaṃ devi mṛtakotthāpanādikam sākinīkulasāmānyaḥ pāśacchedaṃ paśugraham  KubjT kurute vividhāścaryaṃ śiraḥsiddho hy anekadhā asiddhasya tu karmāṇi karmayogād vadāmy aham  KubjT aśaktah sādhane vīras tasyedaṃ dveṣaṇaṃ prati śiroruhasamutpannā caṇḍālī juṣṭapūrvikā  KubjT rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu sā dūtī śāsane sampratiṣṭhitā paṭhanād eva saṃsiddhā japahomavivarjitā  KubjT śiraso vaśagā dūtī tadājñā nigrahātmikā  KubjT  oṃ hāsvā ṭpha  hūṃ  sagra  yaramā kaṃmua  capa  madha  hada  naha ṇiridhāṅgaṭvākhalapāka ṇikṣabhasamāṃradhiru līṇḍācāṣṭaju tivagabha  mona oṃ  KubjT  vilomena kṛtābhyāsam uddhared upadeśataḥ sampūjya yoginīṣaṭkaṃ rāmaṇīśirasānvitam  KubjT dāgham utpādayet prathamaṃ lekhya mātrā na saṃśayaḥ ṣaḍasrapuramadhyasthaṃ rakāraṃ tu adhordhvataḥ  KubjT rakāraṃ tu tad evaṃ syād bahiṣkoṇe pṛthak pṛthak ṣaṭprakāraṃ pradātavyaṃ jvālāsañchannalāñchitam  KubjT kopakāle samutpanne citivastre nṛcarmaje likhitavyaṃ sakruddhena viṣonmattarasena ca  KubjT śmaśānāṅgārasaṃyuktaṃ sādhyanāmaṃ tu madhyataḥ likhitvā tāpayet paścāj jvaro bhavati dāruṇaḥ  KubjT jvaram utpādayitvā tu sadantam ānayec chiraḥ pūrvadravyair likhitvā tu nāma tasya gale kṣipet  KubjT viparītamukhaṃ kṛtvā ūrdhvagrīvaṃ yathā bhavet tathā saṃsthāpayed bhūmau kapālaṃ mantravit sudhīḥ  KubjT śmaśāne vā nadītīre kṛtvā vedīṃ tadūrdhvataḥ paścād dhomaṃ prakurvīta ugradravyaiḥ samāhitaḥ  KubjT viṣeṇa gandhakenaiva kunaṭyā tālakena ca rājikālavaṇenaiva nimbapattrais trisaptakam  KubjT prathame hani chāgāntraṃ raktāktaṃ homayed budhaḥ paścād dhyānaṃ prakurvīta kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ sudāruṇam  KubjT jvalantaṃ pādasandhīni mastakāntaṃ vicintayet rakāraṃ tu lalāṭasthaṃ japen mantraṃ punaḥ punaḥ  KubjT homamaṇḍalakaṃ yac ca caturasraṃ vajralāñchitam evaṃ vai bhavate kālo yadi sākṣāt sacīpatiḥ  KubjT evaṃ nigraham ākhyātaṃ śirodevyāḥ samudbhavam caṇḍālīti prayogo yaṃ gopitavyaṃ prayatnataḥ  KubjT śāsanasya ca yo dveṣṭā yo dveṣṭā guravopari teṣv amoghinī cāṇḍālī yojayet paramārthataḥ  KubjT lakṣameke kṛte jāpye vācāmātreṇa mārayet atorthaṃ gopayed devi siddhājñāmoghacaṇḍikā  KubjT śirodūtī parā hy eṣā kṣudrakarmasv anekadhā sarvaṃ svacchandadeveśī kariṣyati śikhojjvalā  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate mantroddhāre ṣaḍaṅgavidyādhikāro nāma saptamaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrīkubjikā uvācaśrutaṃ deva mayākhyātam aśeṣārthasuvistaram kathaṃ devyāḥ śikhāsaṃsthā svacchandaḥ katirūpadhṛk  KubjT prayogavipulaṃ deva sarvopāyavivarjitam adhunāśrotum icchāmi sārāt sārataraṃ vibho  KubjT āpyāyanaṃ śarīrasya ākāśādiprasādhanam arcanaṃ caiva saṅkṣepād grahamardakaraṃ yathā  KubjT ripumardakaraṃ caiva bilayantraprasādhanam jvaraduṣṭaviṣādīnāṃ sarvaduḥkhavimardanam  KubjT yathā smaraṇamātreṇa vyādhito mucyate kṣaṇāt dharmakāmārthasaṃsiddham arthamokṣaprasādhanam  KubjT vaśīkaraṇakarmāṇi ākarṣaṇavidhikriyā divyādivyeṣu kāryeṣu nāgakāryeṣu bhairava  KubjT śarīrasthaṃ yathā brūhi nāḍisthaṃ mudrayā saha saṅkṣepārcanakarma ca saṃsiddhaṃ bhogasādhanam  KubjT vratayāgavihīnaṃ ca vittopāyavivarjitam smaraṇāt kevalo mantraḥ sukham utpādayed yathā  KubjT śrībhairava uvācasādhu kubjini bhadre tvaṃ kathayataḥ śṛṇuṣva me śikhā guṇakalā yasya svacchandasyāmitadyuteḥ  KubjT kubjikāyāḥ śikhā raudrā raudrasiddhipradāyikā sārāt sārataraṃ devi satyaṃ satyaṃ na cānyathā  KubjT aghorān na paro mantraḥ kasmāc cūlīgatas tu saḥ śamanaṃ sarvaduḥkhānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ ca nikṛntanam  KubjT sarvānugrahakaṃ devi bhuktimuktipradāyakam kālanirṇāśanaṃ devi jarāsiṃham udāhṛtam  KubjT dāridraśamanaṃ cedam acireṇa gaṇāmbike āśāḥ saṃśodhayitvā tu devyā nyāsaṃ hi pūrvavat  KubjT hṛdayādiprabhedena astrāntaṃ yāvadāvadhim svasthānanyāsavinyāsaṃ pūrvavac ca yathāsthitam  KubjT śikhāsvacchandadeveśaṃ mantredaṃ pārameśvaram ṣaḍaṅgayajanād vātha nirācāreṇa sidhyati  KubjT tato mudrāṃ parāṃ baddhvā cintayed yonimadhyagām mahāmudreti vikhyātā nākhyātā kasyacin mayā  KubjT dhyātvā pretaṃ purā devi sarvakāraṇakāraṇam mahāyogī mahāsiddhaḥ sarvalokadharaḥ prabhuḥ  KubjT sarvajñaguṇasaṃyuktaṃ padmaṃ tasyopari sthitam karṇikopari dīpyantaṃ prajvalantaṃ mahaujasam  KubjT anantaṃ tad vijānīyāt tasyordhve tacchikhāśivam aṣṭapattrāsanāsīnaṃ dvātriṃśārcibhir āvṛtam  KubjT nānālaṅkārasampannaṃ nānāvarṇaṃ vicintayet daśabāhuṃ mahāghoraṃ caturvaktraṃ sulālasam  KubjT sarvavarṇadharaṃ devam atha śyāmaṃ vincintayet kapālaṃ caiva khaṭvāṅgam anyat paraśuśūladhṛk  KubjT ḍamaruṃ cākṣamālāṃ ca phalaṃ haste niveśayet gajacarmadharau cobhau hastau tu parikīrtitau  KubjT garjantaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ nādaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam bhakṣantaṃ cintayed vyādhiṃ viśveśvarakujeśvaram  KubjT khādyamānāṃ raṭantīṃ tāṃ tāḍyamānāṃ vibheditām bhedayantīṃ triśūlena chedayantīṃ mahāsinā  KubjT kruddhabhāvād dhunantīṃ tāṃ pūrvavyādhiṃ vicintayet tasyopari tam aikāram īśatattvāvadhisthitam  KubjT śikhāsvacchandadeveśaṃ tat sthāpyopari pūjayet svakīyāṅgasamudbhūtam ekavīrāṅgapañcakam  KubjT āgneyyāṃ hṛdayaṃ nyasya śiras tv īśānagocare śikhāṃ śikhātmakāṃ rakṣe tanutrāṇaṃ tu vāyave  KubjT astraṃ diśāsu vinyasya bhūyo madhye prapūjayet juṣṭacaṇḍeśvaraṃ kṣetre pūjādau vighnarāṭ kule  KubjT calādīnām adhiṣṭhānaṃ jānīyād gurupaṅktivat dhūpacandananaivedyaṃ trayāṇāṃ prathamaṃ dadet  KubjT siddhisādhanayuktasya mārgo yaṃ hy avicārakaḥ nirācārapadasthānāṃ kṣetracaṇḍīśavighnarāṭ  KubjT balipūjāsu naivedyaṃ trayāṇāṃ prathamaṃ dadet paścāt kramasya kubjīśe ataḥ śāṭhyaṃ na kārayet  KubjT pāramparyakramaṃ pūjya paścān maṇḍalakopari śikhāsvacchandadeveśaṃ yāmalaṃ tu catuṣkalam  KubjT hṛttanutrāṇaparyantaṃ yajed devaṃ catuṣkalam yogamārgāvalambānāṃ śrīsiddhākhyaṃ catuṣkalam  KubjT pūjya svacchandadeveśaṃ kramāgre maṇḍalopari tato japec chikhānātham aghoraṃ parameśvaram  KubjT praṇavādyaṃ namaskāram asiddhānāṃ niyuñjayet siddhārthayogayuktānām aiṃpādādyantayojitam  KubjT tato  gnipūjanaṃ kṛtvā yathā pūjā tathāhutim sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vātha pañcāśat pañcaviṃśa vā  KubjT tilair homaṃ prakurvīta dadhimadhvājyasaṃyutaiḥ ghṛtasaktvā ca madhunā sarvaduḥkhapramardakam  KubjT vyādhinirṇāśanaṃ kubji śeṣahomaṃ tu bhūtidam sahasreṇa mahābhūtiḥ śatena vyādhināśanam  KubjT śatam aṣṭaśataṃ kubji devatulyo bhaviṣyati sarvaduḥkhavinirmuktaṃ japapūjāsamanvitam  KubjT śatato  ṣṭasahasreṇa triṣkālena tu sundari ṣaṇmāsāj jāyate siddhiḥ sākṣāt paśyati bhairavīm  KubjT yatheṣṭaṃ jāyate siddhir nāsty atramanṛtaṃ vacaḥ sahasreṇa jvaraṃ yāti chāgasya piśitair hutaiḥ  KubjT triṣkālaṃ māsam ekaṃ tu sahasraṃ hunate tu saḥ sidhyate māṃsahomena kṣaudrājyadadhisaṃyutam  KubjT yavakṣīrānnahomena śālitaṇḍulasādhitam prīyate tu śikhādevaḥ svacchando ghorarūpadhṛk  KubjT dadhihomāt parā puṣṭiḥ kṣīrahomena śāntikam ṣaṇmāsāt tu ghṛtaṃ hutvā sarvavyādhivināśanam  KubjT rājayakṭmaṃ tilair homād āyuvṛddhir yavair hutaiḥ kuṣṭhasyaiva sadā homāt triyuktais taṇḍulaiḥ priye  KubjT samasaktughṛtenāśu nāśayeta bhagandaram tilair homaṃ prakurvīta dadhimadhvājyasaṃyutam  KubjT vyādhinirṇāśanaṃ kubji śeṣahomas tu bhūtidaḥ ghṛtakevalahomena sarvavyādhinikṛntanam  KubjT prayogaṃ sampravakṣyāmi yad uktaṃ te purā mayā dharmakāmārthamokṣāṇāṃ caturvargaphalodayam  KubjT tava kubji pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvekamanādhunā sarvavyādhiharaṃ dhyānaṃ paraṃ puṣṭivivardhanam  KubjT āśāṃ saṃśodhayet pūrvaṃ nyāsaṃ kṛtvā tu pūrvakam pūrvaṃ nyasya ca mantreśaṃ nāḍīvarṇais tathākṣaraiḥ  KubjT adhaḥsrotaṃ tu vāmena dakṣiṇordhvagataṃ priye nyāsaṃ kṛtvā śarīre tu mantrarājam anusmaret  KubjT pañcapraṇavamādyena aghoreṇa surādhipe adhyuṣṭamātrād uttīrṇaṃ jñātvā mantram anusmaret  KubjT akulāditrimadhyasthaṃ kulāc cādes trimadhyagam madhyamāditrimadhyasthaṃ piṇḍādes tu trimadhyagam  KubjT trayārdhamātrasaṃyuktaṃ praṇavedaṃ śikhāśivam trināḍīpiṇḍasambhūtaṃ mudrayā cordhvadīpitam  KubjT tripakṣakṣayakartāraṃ tridhābaddhaṃ triśūlinam trimūrtiguṇasambhūtaṃ tenāsau tridaśeśvaraḥ  KubjT trimārgavihitaṃ śāntaṃ tripathāntasamudbhavam tripathena vinā bhadre bhrājate yonimaṇḍalam  KubjT yoniṃ vinā na niṣpattir divyādivyeṣu vastuṣu uttamottamamadhyasthā kanyasāntavyavasthitā  KubjT bindu śaktis tathā nādaṃ mātrātrayam udāhṛtam trayāṇām api saṃyogān niṣpadyeta bhagālayam  KubjT parārdhamātrasambhinnaṃ praṇavo yaṃ kulāgame aumakārasaṃyuktaṃ praṇavedaṃ kriyātmakam  KubjT sādākhyeśvararudrāṇāṃ brahmaviṣṇuranukramāt ete te praṇavāḥ pañca kriyākāraṇagocare  KubjT praṇavādisamudbhūtāḥ pañcaite guṇavattarāḥ pañcapraṇavamādyantaṃ tatordhve tu śikhāśivam  KubjT evaṃ tu praṇavaṃ divyaṃ sugopyaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam atra devi sphuṭaṃ tubhyaṃ bhrāntaṃ cātra jagattrayam  KubjT jñātvevaṃ saṃsmared yas tu sannidhāno sti tasya vai sudurlabhaḥ prayogo yaṃ guruvaktrāt tu labhyate  KubjT yatrotpannaṃ tato yāti layaṃ kṛtvā surādhipe utpattipralayaṃ jñātvā tato mantram anusmaret  KubjT yat kiñcit kurute kāryaṃ sādhakaḥ sādhanātmakaḥ uccaret tu layāntasthaṃ tarjanyāgre vyavasthitam  KubjT nāḍīsūtreṇa vinyastaṃ bahir ante ca mātaraḥ yā nāḍī sā bhaved varṇas tayā nāḍyā tu veṣṭayet  KubjT yadi candraṃ vahec cakraṃ sūryaṃ vā cakram uttamam tasya madhye svayaṃ sthitvā viśvo ham iti cintayet  KubjT ahaṃ brahmā tathā viṣṇur ahaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ bhairavo ham iti devi cintayitvā tu sādhakaḥ  KubjT hṛnmadhye cintayec cakraṃ nāḍīvarṇais tathākṣaraiḥ ādyakṣaraṃ japen mantraṃ punar ādyaṃ niyojayet  KubjT evaṃ saṃsmṛtya vidhivat sarvakarmāṇi sādhayet arcanaṃ havanaṃ dhyānaṃ japam ekāntarūpiṇam  KubjT karma kṛtvā kujeśāni kujeśāya nivedayet tato dhyānaṃ prakurvīta viśuddhenāntarātmanā  KubjT sa eva mantram uccārya ādyādau yāvad antimam nādena tu gatiṃ kuryāt svacchandagatibhāvitaḥ  KubjT brahmaṃ bhittvā tato viṣṇuṃ rudram īśvaram eva ca setumadhyena gamanaṃ kuñcikodghāṭayed bilam  KubjT udghāṭya paramaṃ sthānam aghoraṃ yatra saṃsthitam aṣṭākapāla ghorīśaṃ tryakṣaraṃ samanusmaret  KubjT sarvamantreṣu hṛdayaṃ yat kubjīśaśikhātmakam manasā smṛtamātreṇa khecaratvaṃ prajāyate  KubjT sarvavighnopaśamanaṃ mantraṃ tryakṣaram uttamam śeṣaṣaṭkaṃ tu yad devi tadaṅgāny asya kalpayet  KubjT japtavyaṃ tu śikhāsūtraṃ sakṛt siddhiḥ prajāyate ākāśādiprasiddhyarthaṃ siddhir anyāsu kā kathā  KubjT mantrasannaddhadehas tu sarvāvastho pi sādhakaḥ tiṣṭhan jāgran svapan gacchan bhuñjāno maithune rataḥ  KubjT caryādhārī nirācāro mantrasaṃsmaraṇāc chuciḥ sāmānyasmaraṇād eva vyādhibhir nābhibhūyate  KubjT prajvalan dṛśyate bhūtair yasyedaṃ tu śarīragam ataḥ kiṃ bahunoktena siṃhasyaiva yathā mṛgāḥ  KubjT gandhena pralayaṃ yānti satyaṃ satyaṃ mahātape japena sādhayet sarvaṃ vratastho yas tu sādhakaḥ  KubjT pūrvam eva japel lakṣaṃ sidhyate ghoramūrdhajam aviditvā vidhānena kiñcit kāryaṃ na sādhayet  KubjT yaḥ kuryād vidhihīnaṃ tu sa vighnaiś cābhibhūyate tasmāt padārthanavakaṃ jñātavyaṃ tu kujeśvari  KubjT kṣetrasthānāni suśroṇi jñātavyāni suniścitaiḥ kṣetraṃ vratāni mantrāś ca akṣasūtraṃ japaṃ tathā  KubjT dhyānaṃ pūjā tathā dravyaṃ varṇaṃ mukhasamanvitam mukhahīnā na sidhyanti agnihotravivarjitāḥ  KubjT mukham āhavanīyaṃ syāt tasmin mantrāḥ sadā sthitāḥ aghoraṃ kālam ity uktam aghoraṃ viṣṇur ucyate  KubjT aghoras tvaṃ maheśāni aghoraś cāham eva ca bahurūpadharo hy agniḥ pracaṇḍaḥ kālamantagaḥ  KubjT sa śivaḥ paramo brahmā nirvāṇaḥ sa sadāśivaḥ īśvaraḥ sa paro nityam asmāt parataro na hi  KubjT anena smṛtamātreṇa sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pramucyate dāridrasiṃho ghorīśo vyādhisiṃhaḥ kuleśvari  KubjT pracaṇḍaduṣṭasiṃhaś ca mahāpātakanāśanaḥ sarvatīrthābhiṣekaś ca saptajaptena jāyate  KubjT śatajaptena devena sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet dīkṣānirvāṇakārī syāt trisaptaparivartanāt  KubjT daśāvartena duritaṃ brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati daśāvartād guropekṣī smaraṇād eva mucyate  KubjT vidhihīne tathā pāne pañcabhiś copapātakī śatena caiva triṣkālyaṃ varṣāt siddhir yathepsitā  KubjT balavatāṃ ripūṇāṃ tu vyastam āvartayet prabhuḥ dakṣiṇāsyo mahādevi sahasreṇa nipātayet  KubjT saṅgrāmakāle smartavyam asipattragataṃ hṛdi veṣṭantaṃ mātṛbhiḥ sainyaṃ bhakṣa bhakṣeti bhāṣayet  KubjT hatadarpāḥ prajāyante na punaḥ saṃharanti ca duḥsvapne dviguṇaṃ jāpyaṃ vraṇe caiva caturguṇam  KubjT lūtā daśaguṇaṃ caiva viṣe vai viṃśatis tathā dine dine śataṃ japtvā vibhūtir vardhate  cirāt  KubjT prāṅmukho yasya nāmnā tu sādhyārūḍho hṛdi sthitaḥ vaśībhavati rājānaṃ śatajāpyena dhīmatā  KubjT saptāhāt sa balopeto vaśībhavati nānyathā dine dine sahasreṇa nāsti tad yan na sādhayet  KubjT ādityābhimukho bhūtvā sahasraṃ parivartayet yat kiñcid vihitaṃ citte saptāhāt sādhayiṣyati  KubjT nyastaṃ sarvāṅgikaṃ mantraṃ bhairavākārasaṃsthitam sa tu bhojanakāle tu pātre sañcintya sādhakaḥ  KubjT sampūrṇaśaśinaṃ dhyāyed bhuñjāno mṛtam aśnute sampūrṇacandramadhyastham adhordhvasampuṭīkṛtam  KubjT paryaṭet sādhako nityaṃ sarvaśreyam avāpnuyāt yad icchet sādhakaḥ siddhiṃ hṛdi kṛtvā kujeśvaram  KubjT candramaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ svacchandagatibhāvitam tatpraviṣṭaṃ vicinteta antyād antaṃ parāparam  KubjT parasparaṃ tu sañcintya yāvad brahmabilaṃ gataḥ  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate svacchandaśikhādhikāro nāmāṣṭamaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrībhairava uvācabhedayitvā paraṃ tattvaṃ hakāraṃ nāma nāmataḥ so ṣṭākapālo vijñeyas tasyākāśaṃ tu tac chiraḥ  KubjT aghoram iti vikhyātaṃ dvātriṃśākṣarabhūṣitam tasmāt sañjāyate sṛṣṭiḥ sā tu sṛṣṭir hṛdi sthitā  KubjT dvātriṃśa mātaras tās tu cakrārūḍhā vicintayet caṇḍā ghaṇṭā mahānāsā sumukhī durmukhī balā  KubjT revatī prathamā ghorā saumyā bhīmā mahābalā jayā ca vijayā caiva ajitā cāparājitā  KubjT mahotkaṭā virūpākṣī śuṣkā cākāśamātarā sehārī jātahārī ca kiñcit tan netrāṅgasamudbhavam asyāṅgasya tu māhātmyaṃ jyotiṣeśvarasāgare  KubjT paramāstrasya madhye tu khādakāstraṃ mahābalam tasya vyāvarṇitaṃ pūrvaṃ tantraṃ svābhāvalakṣaṇam  KubjT abhiṣekaṃ vāmajaṅghāsamāyuktaṃ nitambālaṅkṛtaṃ priye etad devyāstraparamaṃ nāpuṇyo labhate sphuṭam  KubjT kramapūjāvidhānena yathāvibhavavistaram dīpamālābhir uddyotaṃ kṛtvā dhūpādhivāsitam  KubjT śaṅkhaṃ vā kalaśaṃ vāpi abhimantrya svavidyayā uttamādhamamadhyasya karmasevānusārataḥ  KubjT tayā vidyābhiṣekaṃ tu nyastavyā kalaśe tu sā śiṣyahaste tu taṃ dattvā idaṃ kūṭaṃ tu yojayet  KubjT yāvat kṣubhyaty asau hastaḥ svayam eva calaty asau dhāraṇād iva saṃyātaṃ yadā patati mastake  KubjT tadā tu jāyate sau vai sādhyalakṣaṇasādhakaḥ dagdhapāpaḥ prajāyeta nātra kāryavicāraṇāt  KubjT nāśiṣyāya pradātavyaṃ na dhūrtāya na nindake bhaktāya śraddadhānāya gurubhaktāya sundari  KubjT tasya deyam idaṃ devi abhiṣekaṃ varānane tadā tu sādhayet karma yad uktaṃ karmasantatau  KubjT  ṭpha  hūṃ  yataghāvi  yataghā siddhā jñātvaitān bhinnadṛṣṭinā sa jānāti varārohe samastāmnāyapaddhatim  KubjT anyathā na bhavet siddhiḥ kiñcijjñaḥ paścimānvaye śrutvā savismayaṃ vākyam ānandapraṇayānvitam  KubjT uvācedaṃ punaḥ kubjī ṣaḍadhvaṃ vada me prabho  KubjT śrībhairava uvācayuktam uktaṃ ca deveśi śrūyatāṃ paramārthataḥ saṅkṣepāt kathayiṣyāmi śeṣānyat purataḥ punaḥ  KubjT bhūtaṃ bhāvaṃ tathā śāktaṃ māntraṃ raudraṃ ca śāmbhavam ājñātaḥ sampravarteta ṣaḍadhvedaṃ kulānvaye  KubjT bhūtaṃ bhuvanāvaraṇaṃ padaṃ bhāvaṃ prayujyate śāktaṃ varṇāḥ samākhyātā māntraṃ dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ  KubjT raudraṃ kalādhvaraṃ proktaṃ śāmbhavaṃ tattvalakṣaṇam ājñānalavatī dīkṣā mantrāṇāṃ sādhane hitā  KubjT sā cājñā pūrvikā siddhā anyathā tilaghātakī sā ca tattvavatāṃ caiva tattvaṃ vai śāmbhavam padam  KubjT tat padaṃ vidyate yasya sāmarthajñaḥ sa sarvaśaḥ jñānamārgaprasiddhyarthaṃ dīkṣā vedhavatī śubhā  KubjT yogyatātaḥ pradātavyā subhaktasya kulādhvare sarvāsām eva dīkṣānāṃ cottamā parikīrtitā  KubjT tena vedho na kartavyo na ṣaḍvidho hy alpasvalpavat pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni cāviśanti ca yasya vai  KubjT bhūtāveśaṃ tu tad viddhi bhāvāveśam ataḥ śṛṇu śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca bhāvajam  KubjT śrotraṃ tvak pañcāvasthā s tu raudrajāḥ anādhītāni śāstrāṇi granthataś cārthataḥ sudhīḥ  KubjT atītānāgataṃ sarvaṃ vartamānasya yat phalam raudraśaktisamāveśāt sarvam eva prapadyate  KubjT yasyedaṃ vartate cihnaṃ śodhitas tu yadā śiśuḥ tadā sampadyate tasya śāmbhavaṃ guṇadāyakam  KubjT kubjīśo yaṃ yadāyātaḥ puṃso janmany apaścime tadā sampadyate tasya śāmbhavaṃ kubjike tanau  KubjT bahvarthakāle pi viśodhitātmā ātmaiva sau paśyati sarvabhūtān na me samāno bhuvanāntarāle viśuddhabhāvo bhavate hy akāle  KubjT ekaikaṃ bhuvanaṃ paśyet puṃsādau conmanāvadhim viśuddhatanujo hy evaṃ dehenānena cotpatet  KubjT na kampadhunane tasya īśadghūrmiḥ pravartate viṣonmūrchāgatas tv evaṃ tiṣṭhate bhūtakumbhavat  KubjT paśyate cāgrataḥ sarvaṃ tattvavrātaṃ sadoditam tatkṣaṇād viṣayān mucyej jīrṇakañcur yathoragaḥ  KubjT sadānandamadonmattaḥ sarvajñaguṇabhūṣitaḥ śāmbhavena tu viddhasya cihnedaṃ sampravartate  KubjT bhūtabhāvanaśaktīnāṃ mantrāveśa ṃ  saraudrajam krameṇa śāmbhavas teṣāṃ viśuddhatvaṃ yathā yathā  KubjT jhalajhaleti yad vedhaṃ sampūrṇaghaṭavad yathā bhūtāntaśaktimantrādau tathedaṃ sampracakṣyate  KubjT gurubhaktivihīnānāṃ vañcakānāṃ yaśasvini pūrvaṃ śāmbhavaviddhasya bhūtādyaṃ vastre vātha suśobhane  KubjT tatopari yajet siddhān sarvajñaguṇaśālinān caturviṃśa ṣoḍaśaivam aṣṭau caiva tripaṅktiṣu  KubjT dvau siddhau madhyadeśe tu kuṅkumena tu cākṣataiḥ trihastaṃ maṇḍalaṃ anyad yat te manasthaṃ tu tat pṛccha vadato mama  KubjT  iti kulālikāmnāye śrīkubjikāmate devyāsamayo nāma mantroddhāre daśamaḥ paṭalaḥ  śrīkubjikā uvācamantratantrais tvayā deva bhrāmitāhaṃ KubjT kalākarmasamāyogāt svādhiṣṭhānaṃ vinirmitam śatakoṭisuvistīrṇaṃ bhuvanānekasaṅkulam  KubjT māyākālakalākīrṇam ādhāraṃ brahmaṇas tu tat catuṣkalasamopetaṃ śivaśaktisamanvitam  KubjT ṣaṭprakāram
